   अत्रोपपत्तिं ते वक्ष्ये शृणु प्राणप्रियेरिताम्‌ ॥ ६१ ॥
   sarvaiḥ jñātaṁ maheśasya niyati-ārabdha-laṅghanam ।
   atra upapattiṁ te vakṣye śṛṇu prāṇa-priyeritām ॥ 61 ॥
   sarvaiḥ — by all; jñātam — known; maheśasya — of Maheśa; niyati — fate; ārabdha — ordained; laṅghanam — transgression; atra — here; upapattiṁ — reasoning; te — to you; vakṣye — I will tell; śṛṇu — listen; prāṇa-priyeritām — dear to life
   It is known by all that Maheśa can transgress ordained fate. I will explain the reasoning behind this; listen, dear to my heart.
   
   Verse 62
   यद्यप्यनुल्लङ्घनीये प्रारब्धनियती खलु ।
   तथाप्यपौरुषाणां तत्‌ प्रारब्धमनपोहनम्‌ ॥ ६२ ॥
   yadyapi anullaṅghanīye prārabdha-niyatī khalu ।
   tathā api apauruṣāṇāṁ tat prārabdhaṁ anapohanam ॥ 62 ॥
   yadyapi — even though; anullaṅghanīye — not to be transgressed; prārabdha — ordained; niyatī — fate; khalu — indeed; tathā — still; api — also; apauruṣāṇām — for the non-determined; tat — that; prārabdhaṁ — fate; anapohanam — not negated
   Even though ordained fate is not to be transgressed, for those lacking determination, that fate remains unaltered.
   
   Verse 63
   अत एव प्राणयमैः प्रारब्धं परिजीयते ।
   न तान्‌ दृष्टेषु दुःखेषु प्रारब्धं योजयत्यलम्‌ ॥ ६३ ॥
   ata eva prāṇayamaiḥ prārabdhaṁ parijīyate ।
   na tān dṛṣṭeṣu duḥkheṣu prārabdhaṁ yojayati alam ॥ 63 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; eva — indeed; prāṇayamaiḥ — through breath control; prārabdhaṁ — fate; parijīyate — is conquered; na — not; tān — them; dṛṣṭeṣu — in seen; duḥkheṣu — sufferings; prārabdhaṁ — fate; yojayati — imposes; alam — sufficiently
   Therefore, through breath control, fate is conquered. It does not impose sufficient suffering on those who are determined; this is observed.
   
   Verse 64
   प्रारब्धाहिनिगीर्णास्ते ये पौरुषपराङ्मुखाः ।
   एतन्नियतिसंक्लृप्तं तथैवानुभवान्ननु ॥ ६४ ॥
   prārabdha-ahi-nigīrṇāḥ te ye pauruṣa-parāṅmukhāḥ ।
   etat niyati-saṁkḷptam tathā eva anubhavān nanu ॥ 64 ॥
   prārabdha-ahi-nigīrṇāḥ — swallowed by the serpent of fate; te — they; ye — who; pauruṣa-parāṅmukhāḥ — lacking determination; etat — this; niyati-saṁkḷptam — designed by fate; tathā — thus; eva — indeed; anubhavān — experience; nanu — indeed
   Those who are swallowed by the serpent of fate, lacking determination, indeed experience it as ordained by fate.
   
   Verse 65
   नियतिः स्यादीशशक्तिः सङ्कल्पैकस्वरूपिणी ।
   सत्यस सङ्कल्प एवेशोऽनुल्लङ्घया ह्यत एव सा ॥ ६५ ॥
   niyatiḥ syāt īśa-śaktiḥ saṅkalpa-eka-svarūpiṇī ।
   satyaḥ saṅkalpaḥ eva īśaḥ anullaṅghayā hi ataḥ eva sā ॥ 65 ॥
   niyatiḥ — fate; syāt — is; īśa-śaktiḥ — power of the lord; saṅkalpa-eka-svarūpiṇī — solely of the nature of will; satyaḥ — true; saṅkalpaḥ — will; eva — indeed; īśaḥ — lord; anullaṅghayā — not to be transgressed; hi — indeed; ataḥ — thus; eva — indeed; sā — she
   Fate is the power of the lord, solely of the nature of his will. The true will of the lord is indeed not to be transgressed.
   
   Verse 66
   कुण्ठिता सापि भवति परमेशपरायणे ।
   अकुण्ठितापि भवति यतः सा तादृशी भवेत्‌ ॥ ६६ ॥
   kuṇṭhitā sā api bhavati parameśa-parāyaṇe ।
   akuṇṭhitā api bhavati yataḥ sā tādṛśī bhavet ॥ 66 ॥
   kuṇṭhitā — hindered; sā — she; api — also; bhavati — becomes; parameśa-parāyaṇe — devoted to the supreme lord; akuṇṭhitā — unhindered; api — also; bhavati — becomes; yataḥ — because; sā — she; tādṛśī — such; bhavet — becomes
   She becomes hindered when devoted to the supreme lord, yet she also becomes unhindered because of that lord.
   
   Verse 67
   तस्मात्‌ कुतर्क सन्त्यज्य महेशं शरणीकुरु ।
   अहेतुकतया स त्वां नियोजयति श्रेयसि ॥ ६७ ॥
   tasmāt kutarka santyajya maheśaṁ śaraṇīkuru ।
   ahetukatayā sa tvāṁ niyojayati śreyasi ॥ 67 ॥
   tasmāt — therefore; kutarka — faulty reasoning; santyajya — abandoning; maheśam — lord Maheśa; śaraṇīkuru — take refuge; ahetukatayā — causelessly; saḥ — he; tvām — you; niyojayati — engages; śreyasi — in welfare
   Therefore, abandon faulty reasoning and take refuge in Lord Maheśa. He will causelessly engage you in welfare.
   
   Verse 68
   एतावदेव सोपानं प्रथमं क्षेमसौधकेः ।
   एतद्विहाय चान्यत्र नास्तीषत्फलसम्भव ॥ ६८ ॥
   etāvata eva sopānaṁ prathamaṁ kṣema-saudhakeḥ ।
   etat vihāya ca anyatra nāsti iṣat-phala-sambhavaḥ ॥ 68 ॥
   etāvataḥ — of this much; eva — indeed; sopānam — step; prathamam — first; kṣema-saudhakeḥ — of the mansion of welfare; etat — this; vihāya — leaving; ca — and; anyatra — elsewhere; nāsti — is not; iṣat-phala-sambhavaḥ — even a little fruit-bearing
   This is indeed the first step to the mansion of welfare. Without taking this step, there is no fruit-bearing elsewhere.
   
   Verse 69
   श्रुत्वेत्थं वचनं राम हेमचूडः प्रियोदितम्‌ ।
   पप्रच्छ भूयस्तां कान्तामतिहृष्टमनास्तदा ॥ ६९ ॥
   śrutvā ittham vacanaṁ rāma hemacūḍaḥ priyoditam ।
   papraccha bhūyas tām kāntām ati-hṛṣṭa-manāḥ tadā ॥ 69 ॥
   śrutvā — having heard; ittham — thus; vacanam — words; rāma — O Rāma; hemacūḍaḥ — Hemachūḍa; priya-uditam — spoken by the beloved; papraccha — asked; bhūyas — again; tām — her; kāntām — dear; ati-hṛṣṭa-manāḥ — with a very pleased mind; tadā — then
   Having heard these words, O Rāma, Hemachūḍa, with a very pleased mind, asked his dear one again.
   
   Verse 70
   प्रिये महेश्वरं ब्रूहि य शरण्यो भवेन्मम ।
   सर्वकर्ता स्वतन्त्रात्मा यच्छक्त्या नियतं जगत्‌ ॥ ७० ॥
   priye maheśvaraṁ brūhi yaḥ śaraṇyaḥ bhavet mama ।
   sarva-kartā svatantra-ātmā yat-śaktyā niyataṁ jagat ॥ 70 ॥
   priye — dear; maheśvaram — Maheśa; brūhi — tell; yaḥ — who; śaraṇyaḥ — refuge; bhavet — becomes; mama — for me; sarva-kartā — creator of all; svatantra-ātmā — independent self; yat-śaktyā — by whose power; niyatam — controlled; jagat — world
   Dear, tell me about Maheśa, who can be my refuge, the creator of all, the independent self, by whose power the world is controlled.
   
   Verse 71
   तं विष्णुमाहुः केचिद्वै शिवमन्ये गणेश्वरम्‌ ।
   तथा सूर्य नृसिंहादीन्‌ बुद्धं सुगतमेव च ॥ ७१ ॥
   taṁ viṣṇum āhuḥ kecid vai śivam anye gaṇeśvaram ।
   tathā sūrya nṛsiṁhādīn buddhaṁ sugatam eva ca ॥ 71 ॥
   tam — him; viṣṇum — Vishnu; āhuḥ — call; kecid — some; vai — indeed; śivam — Shiva; anye — others; gaṇeśvaram — Ganesha; tathā — also; sūrya — Surya; nṛsiṁha-ādīn — Narasimha and others; buddham — Buddha; sugatam — Sugata; eva — indeed; ca — and
   Some call him Vishnu, others call him Shiva, Ganesha, Surya, Narasimha, Buddha, or Sugata.
   
   Verse 72
   अर्हन्तं वासुदेवं च प्राणं सोमं च पावकम्‌ ।
   कर्म प्रधानमणव इत्यादि बहुधा जगुः ॥ ७२ ॥
   arhantaṁ vāsudevaṁ ca prāṇaṁ somaṁ ca pāvakam ।
   karma pradhānam aṇava iti ādi bahudhā jaguḥ ॥ 72 ॥
   arhantam — Arhant; vāsudevam — Vasudeva; ca — and; prāṇam — Prana; somam — Soma; ca — and; pāvakam — Pavaka; karma — action; pradhānam — the main principle; aṇava — atoms; iti — thus; ādi — etc.; bahudhā — in many ways; jaguḥ — said
   They have called him Arhant, Vasudeva, Prana, Soma, Pavaka, and described him in many ways as action, the main principle, and atoms.
   
   Verse 73
   जगत्कारणरूपं वै विचित्रमतभेदितम्‌ ।
   तत्र क्वेश्वरबुद्धिस्तु कर्तव्या तत्‌ समीरय ॥ ७३ ॥
   jagat-kāraṇa-rūpaṁ vai vicitra-mata-bheditam ।
   tatra kva īśvara-buddhiḥ tu kartavyā tat samīraya ॥ 73 ॥
   jagat-kāraṇa-rūpam — form of the world's cause; vai — indeed; vicitra-mata-bheditam — divided by various beliefs; tatra — there; kva — where; īśvara-buddhiḥ — understanding of the lord; tu — but; kartavyā — should be done; tat — that; samīraya — consider
   The form of the world's cause is divided by various beliefs. In this context, where should one place their understanding of the lord?
   
   Verse 74
   नते ह्यविदितं किञ्चिद्‌ भवेदिति हि निश्चयः ।
   यतः स भगवान्‌ व्याघ्रपादो दृष्टपरावरः ॥ ७४ ॥
   nate hi aviditaṁ kiñcit bhavet iti hi niścayaḥ ।
   yataḥ sa bhagavān vyāghrapādaḥ dṛṣṭa-parāvaraḥ ॥ 74 ॥
   nate — to you; hi — indeed; aviditam — unknown; kiñcit — anything; bhavet — may be; iti — thus; hi — indeed; niścayaḥ — certainty; yataḥ — because; saḥ — he; bhagavān — the lord; vyāghrapādaḥ — Vyāghrapāda; dṛṣṭa-parāvaraḥ — seen the past and future
   It is clear that nothing is unknown to you, as the lord Vyāghrapāda, who has seen both the past and the future, has stated this.
   
   Verse 75
   अतस्ते योषितोऽप्येवं ज्ञानमेतद्विराजते ।
   ब्रूहि मे श्रद्दधानाय प्रियायामृतभाषिणि ॥ ७५ ॥
   ataḥ te yoṣitaḥ api evaṁ jñānam etat virājate ।
   brūhi me śraddadhānāya priyāyāmṛta-bhāṣiṇi ॥ 75 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; te — your; yoṣitaḥ — women; api — also; evam — thus; jñānam — knowledge; etat — this; virājate — shines; brūhi — tell; me — to me; śraddadhānāya — faithful; priyā — dear; amṛta-bhāṣiṇi — nectar-speaking
   Therefore, you too, women, shine with this knowledge. Tell me, dear one who speaks with nectar-like words, with faithfulness.
   
   Verse 76
   पृष्टैवं सा हेमलेखा प्रियेण प्राह हर्षिता ।
   नाथ ते सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि शृण्वीश्वरविनिर्णयम्‌ ॥ ७६ ॥
   pṛṣṭā evaṁ sā hemalekhā priyena prāha harṣitā ।
   nātha te sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇu īśvara-vinirṇayam ॥ 76 ॥
   pṛṣṭā — asked; evaṁ — thus; sā — she; hemalekhā — Hemalekha; priyena — by her dear; prāha — said; harṣitā — delighted; nātha — lord; te — to you; sampravakṣyāmi — will explain; śṛṇu — listen; īśvara-vinirṇayam — decision about the lord
   Thus asked, Hemalekha, delighted, said to her dear, "Lord, I will explain. Listen to the decision about the supreme being."
   
   Verse 77
   ईश्वरो हि जगज्जालप्रलयोत्पादकृद्‌ भवेत्‌ ।
   स विष्णुः स शिवो धाता स सूर्यः सोम एव च ॥ ७७ ॥
   īśvaraḥ hi jagat-jāla-pralaya-utpāda-kṛt bhavet ।
   sa viṣṇuḥ sa śivaḥ dhātā sa sūryaḥ soma eva ca ॥ 77 ॥
   īśvaraḥ — lord; hi — indeed; jagat-jāla — universe; pralaya — dissolution; utpāda-kṛt — creator; bhavet — is; saḥ — he; viṣṇuḥ — Vishnu; saḥ — he; śivaḥ — Shiva; dhātā — creator; saḥ — he; sūryaḥ — Surya; soma — Soma; eva — indeed; ca — and
   The lord is indeed the creator and dissolver of the universe. He is Vishnu, Shiva, the creator, Surya, and Soma.
   
   Verse 78
   स एव सर्वथा सर्वः सर्वैरपि निरूपितः ।
   न शिवो नापि विष्णुर्वा न धाता नान्य एव च ॥ ७८ ॥
   saḥ eva sarvathā sarvaḥ sarvaiḥ api nirūpitaḥ ।
   na śivaḥ na api viṣṇuḥ vā na dhātā na anya eva ca ॥ 78 ॥
   saḥ — he; eva — indeed; sarvathā — in every way; sarvaḥ — all; sarvaiḥ — by all; api — also; nirūpitaḥ — designated; na — not; śivaḥ — Shiva; na — not; api — even; viṣṇuḥ — Vishnu; vā — or; na — not; dhātā — creator; na — not; anyaḥ — another; eva — indeed; ca — and
   He is indeed all-encompassing and designated by many names. He is neither Shiva, Vishnu, nor the creator, nor any other specific form.
   
   Verse 79
   एतत्ते सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि शृण्वत्यन्तसमाहितः ।
   कर्तारं शिवमाहुस्ते पञ्चवक्त्रं त्रिलोचनम्‌ ॥ ७९ ॥
   etat te sampravakṣyāmi śṛṇu ati-samāhitaḥ ।
   kartāraṁ śivam āhuḥ te pañca-vaktraṁ tri-locanam ॥ 79 ॥
   etat — this; te — to you; sampravakṣyāmi — will explain; śṛṇu — listen; ati-samāhitaḥ — very focused; kartāram — creator; śivam — Shiva; āhuḥ — they say; te — they; pañca-vaktram — five-faced; tri-locanam — three-eyed
   I will explain this to you; listen closely. They say that Shiva, the five-faced and three-eyed one, is the creator.
   
   Verse 80
   स कर्ता घटकर्तेव चेतनः सशरीरकः ।
   लोकेऽपि चेतनः कर्ता सशरीरो हि दृश्यते ॥ ८० ॥
   saḥ kartā ghaṭa-kartā iva cetanaḥ sa-śarīrakaḥ ।
   loke api cetanaḥ kartā sa-śarīraḥ hi dṛśyate ॥ 80 ॥
   saḥ — he; kartā — creator; ghaṭa-kartā iva — like a potter; cetanaḥ — conscious; sa-śarīrakaḥ — with a body; loke — in the world; api — also; cetanaḥ — conscious; kartā — creator; sa-śarīraḥ — with a body; hi — indeed; dṛśyate — is seen
   He is the creator, like a conscious potter with a body. Similarly, in the world, a conscious creator with a body is also observed.
   
   Verse 81
   अशरीरोऽचेतनो वा न कर्ता क्वचिदीक्षितः ।
   तत्र मुख्यं हि कर्तृत्वं चेतनस्यैव सम्भवेत्‌ ॥ ८१ ॥
   aśarīro'cetano vā na kartā kvacidīkṣitaḥ ।
   tatra mukhyaṁ hi kartṛtvaṁ cetanasyaiva sambhavet ॥ 81 ॥
   aśarīraḥ — bodiless; acetanaḥ — unconscious; vā — or; na — not; kartā — doer; kvacit — anywhere; īkṣitaḥ — observed; tatra — there; mukhyam — principal; hi — indeed; kartṛtvam — doership; cetanasya — of the conscious; eva — only; sambhavet — is possible
   A bodiless or unconscious entity is never observed as a doer anywhere. Therefore, true doership is only possible for the conscious.
   
   Verse 82
   यतः स्वप्नेष्वयं जीवो हित्वा स्थूल शरीरकम्‌ ।
   चैतन्यमयदेहेन सर्वानभिमतान्‌ सृजेत्‌ ॥ ८२ ॥
   yataḥ svapneṣvayaṁ jīvo hitvā sthūla śarīrakam ।
   caitanyamaya-dehena sarvān abhimatān sṛjet ॥ 82 ॥
   yataḥ — because; svapneṣu — in dreams; ayam — this; jīvaḥ — soul; hitvā — leaving; sthūla śarīrakam — gross body; caitanya-maya-dehena — with a body of consciousness; sarvān — all; abhimatān — desired; sṛjet — creates
   In dreams, the soul, leaving the gross body, creates all desired things with a body of consciousness.
   
   Verse 83
   अतः शरीरं करणं कार्ये कर्तुश्चिदात्मनः ।
   जीवानां करणापेक्षा यतोऽपूर्णा स्वतन्त्रता ॥ ८३ ॥
   ataḥ śarīraṁ karaṇaṁ kārye kartuścidātmanaḥ ।
   jīvānāṁ karaṇāpekṣā yato'pūrṇā svatantratā ॥ 83 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; śarīram — body; karaṇam — instrument; kārye — in action; kartuḥ — of the doer; cit-ātmanaḥ — of the conscious self; jīvānām — of living beings; karaṇa-apekṣā — dependence on instruments; yataḥ — because; apūrṇā — incomplete; svatantratā — independence
   Therefore, the body is an instrument for the actions of the conscious self. Since living beings depend on instruments, their independence is incomplete.
   
   Verse 84
   भगवांस्तु जगत्कर्ता पूर्णस्वातन्त्र्ययोगतः ।
   अनपेक्ष्यैव यत्किञ्चित्‌ सृजत्यविकलं जगत्‌ ॥ ८४ ॥
   bhagavāṁstu jagatkartā pūrṇasvātantryayogataḥ ।
   anapekṣyaiva yatkiñcit sṛjatyavikalaṁ jagat ॥ 84 ॥
   bhagavān — the Lord; tu — indeed; jagatkartā — creator of the world; pūrṇa-svātantrya-yogataḥ — due to complete independence; anapekṣya — without depending; eva — indeed; yatkiñcit — anything; sṛjati — creates; avikalam — without deficiency; jagat — world
   Indeed, the Lord, the creator of the world, due to His complete independence, creates everything without depending on anything and without any deficiency.
   
   Verse 85
   अतः शरीरं नास्त्येव ह्येष मुख्यविनिश्चयः ।
   अन्यथा लोकवत्कर्तुरुपादानाश्रयो भवेत्‌ ॥ ८५ ॥
   ataḥ śarīraṁ nāstyeva hyeṣa mukhya-viniścayaḥ ।
   anyathā lokavat karturupādāna-āśrayo bhavet ॥ 85 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; śarīram — body; na asti — does not exist; eva — indeed; hi — indeed; eṣaḥ — this; mukhya-viniścayaḥ — principal conclusion; anyathā — otherwise; lokavat — like the world; kartuḥ — of the doer; upādāna-āśrayaḥ — dependence on material cause; bhavet — would be
   Therefore, the body does not truly exist; this is the main conclusion. Otherwise, like the world, the doer would be dependent on a material cause.
   
   Verse 86
   तथा च देशकालादिकारणप्रचयैर्युतः ।
   जगत्‌ सृजन्महेशानो जीव एव भवेत्तथा ॥ ८६ ॥
   tathā ca deśa-kāla-ādikāraṇa-pracayair-yutaḥ ।
   jagat sṛjan-maheśāno jīva eva bhavet tathā ॥ 86 ॥
   tathā — thus; ca — and; deśa — place; kāla — time; ādi — etc.; kāraṇa-pracayaiḥ — by the collection of causes; yutaḥ — associated; jagat — world; sṛjan — creating; maheśānaḥ — Lord; jīvaḥ — living being; eva — indeed; bhavet — would become; tathā — thus
   Thus, if the Lord were to create the world through a collection of causes such as place and time, He would indeed become a living being.
   
   Verse 87
   पूर्णैश्वर्यं विहन्येत जगत्सृष्टेः पुरापि च ।
   सिद्धयेत्तत्सर्वकर्तृत्वं विहतं स्यान्न संशयः ॥ ८७ ॥
   pūrṇaiśvaryaṁ vihanyeta jagat-sṛṣṭeḥ purā api ca ।
   siddhyet tat sarva-kartṛtvaṁ vihataṁ syān na saṁśayaḥ ॥ 87 ॥
   pūrṇa-aiśvaryam — complete sovereignty; vihanyeta — would be destroyed; jagat-sṛṣṭeḥ — in the creation of the world; purā — earlier; api — also; ca — and; siddhyet — would be accomplished; tat — that; sarva-kartṛtvam — doership of all; vihataṁ — obstructed; syāt — would be; na — not; saṁśayaḥ — doubt
   Complete sovereignty in the creation of the world as earlier discussed would have to be compromised. The doership of all would be obstructed; there is no doubt.
   
   Verse 88
   अतो हि दृश्यदेहाद्यमनपेक्ष्य जगत्‌ सृजेत्‌ ।
   नास्ति तस्मात्‌ स्थूलदेहो वस्तुतः प्राणवल्लभ ॥ ८८ ॥
   ataḥ hi dṛśya-deha-ādyam-anapekṣya jagat sṛjet ।
   nāsti tasmāt sthūla-dehaḥ vastutaḥ prāṇa-vallabha ॥ 88 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; hi — indeed; dṛśya-deha-ādyam — visible body; anapekṣya — without depending; jagat — world; sṛjet — creates; nāsti — does not exist; tasmāt — therefore; sthūla-dehaḥ — gross body; vastutaḥ — in reality; prāṇa-vallabha — beloved of life
   Therefore, the world is created without depending on a visible body. Thus, the gross body does not exist in reality, my beloved of life.
   
   Verse 89
   पररूपे ह्यदेहेऽस्मिन्‌ मुह्यन्ति स्थूलबुद्धयः ।
   भक्तियुक्ताश्च तैर्ध्यातो यत्र यत्र यथा यथा ॥ ८९ ॥
   para-rūpe hi adehe asmin muhyanti sthūla-buddhayaḥ ।
   bhakti-yuktāḥ ca taiḥ dhyātaḥ yatra yatra yathā yathā ॥ 89 ॥
   para-rūpe — in the supreme form; hi — indeed; adehe — bodiless; asmin — in this; muhyanti — are deluded; sthūla-buddhayaḥ — gross-minded; bhakti-yuktāḥ — devoted; ca — and; taiḥ — by them; dhyātaḥ — meditated upon; yatra yatra — wherever; yathā yathā — however
   In the supreme form, the gross-minded are indeed deluded by this bodiless aspect. However, those who are devoted and meditate, regardless of where and how, are not.
   
   Verse 90
   तथा धत्तेऽनेकरूपं भक्तचिन्तामणिः स्वयम्‌ ।
   अतश्चेतन एवेशस्तद्देहः स्याच्चितिः परा ॥ ९० ॥
   tathā dhatte aneka-rūpaṁ bhakta-cintāmaṇiḥ svayam ।
   ataḥ cetanaḥ eva īśaḥ tat-dehaḥ syāt citiḥ parā ॥ 90 ॥
   tathā — thus; dhatte — assumes; aneka-rūpam — many forms; bhakta-cintāmaṇiḥ — wish-fulfilling gem for devotees; svayam — itself; ataḥ — therefore; cetanaḥ — conscious; eva — indeed; īśaḥ — Lord; tat-dehaḥ — his body; syāt — would be; citiḥ parā — supreme consciousness
   Thus, like the wish-fulfilling gem for devotees, the lord takes on many forms. Therefore, the Lord is indeed conscious, and his body must be supreme consciousness.
   
   Verse 91
   चितिरेव महासत्ता सम्राज्ञी परमेश्वरी ।
   त्रिपुरा भासते यस्यामविभिन्न विभिन्नवत्‌ ॥ ९१ ॥
   citiḥ eva mahā-sattā samrājñī parameśvarī ।
   tripurā bhāsate yasyām avibhinna vibhinnavat ॥ 91 ॥
   citiḥ — consciousness; eva — indeed; mahā-sattā — great existence; samrājñī — empress; parameśvarī — supreme goddess; tripurā — Tripura; bhāsate — shines; yasyām — in whom; avibhinna — undivided; vibhinnavat — as divided
   Consciousness is indeed the great existence, the supreme goddess. Tripura shines as the undivided essence from which this world, though appearing divided, emanates.
   
   Verse 92
   आदर्शनगरप्रख्यं जगदेतच्चराचरम्‌ ।
   तद्रूपैकत्वतस्तत्र नोत्तमाधमभावना ॥ ९२ ॥
   ādarśana-nagara-prakhyaṁ jagat etat carācaram ।
   tad-rūpa-ekatvataḥ tatra na uttama-adhamabhāvanā ॥ 92 ॥
   ādarśana-nagara-prakhyam — like the city of illusion; jagat — world; etat — this; carācaram — moving and non-moving; tad-rūpa-ekatvataḥ — due to the oneness of its form; tatra — there; na — not; uttama-adhamabhāvanā — notion of high and low
   This world, both moving and non-moving, is like an illusory city. Its singular form removes any notion of high or low.
   
   Verse 93
   अपरे तु स्वरूपे हि कल्पितं मुख्यतादि हि ।
   तस्मात्‌ प्राज्ञ उपासीत पर रूप हि निष्कलम्‌ ॥ ९३ ॥
   apare tu svarūpe hi kalpitaṁ mukhyatādi hi ।
   tasmāt prājña upāsīta para rūpa hi niṣkalam ॥ 93 ॥
   apare — others; tu — indeed; svarūpe — in the form; hi — indeed; kalpitaṁ — imagined; mukhyatā-ādi — primary etc.; hi — indeed; tasmāt — therefore; prājñaḥ — wise one; upāsīta — should worship; para rūpa — supreme form; hi — indeed; niṣkalam — without parts
   Others may imagine primary and secondary forms; therefore, the wise should worship the supreme, indivisible form.
   
   Verse 94
   असमर्थः स्थूलरूपं यद्‌ बुद्धौ सङ्गतं दृढम्‌ ।
   तदुपास्याहेतुतस्तु श्रेयः प्राप्नोत्यनुत्तमम्‌ ।
   नान्यथास्य गतिः क्वापि भवेद्वै कोटिजन्मभिः ॥ ९४ ॥
   asamarthaḥ sthūla-rūpaṁ yad buddhi saṅgataṁ dṛḍham ।
   tad upāsya ahetutaḥ tu śreyaḥ prāpnoti anuttamam ।
   na anyathā asya gatiḥ kvāpi bhavet vai koṭi janmabhiḥ ॥ 94 ॥
   asamarthaḥ — incapable; sthūla-rūpaṁ — gross form; yad — which; buddhi — intellect; saṅgataṁ — attached; dṛḍham — firmly; tad — that; upāsya — worshiping; ahetutaḥ — without reason; tu — indeed; śreyaḥ — ultimate good; prāpnoti — attains; anuttamam — unsurpassed; na — not; anyathā — otherwise; asya — his; gatiḥ — path; kvāpi — anywhere; bhavet — would be; vai — indeed; koṭi janmabhiḥ — in millions of births
   One whose intellect is fixated on the gross form is limited. By worshiping that form without understanding, he may still attain the ultimate good. Otherwise, his path would remain unfulfilled, even across millions of lifetimes.


   
   इति श्रीमज्ज्ञानखण्डे हेमचूडोपाख्याने ईश्वरस्वरूपनिरूप सप्तमोऽध्यायः ॥
   
   Thus ends the seventh chapter named "Description of the Nature of God" in the Story of Hemachuda in the revered Knowledge Section.


8. EXPLANATION OF DESCRIPTION OF THE WORLD
   Verse 1
   एवं प्रियावचः श्रुत्वा ज्ञात्वा तत्वं महेशितुः ।
   त्रैपुरं चिन्मयं हेमलेखावाक्येन निश्चितम्‌ ॥ १ ॥
   evaṁ priyāvacaḥ śrutvā jñātvā tattvaṁ maheśituḥ ।
   traipuraṁ cinmayaṁ hemalekhāvākyena niścitam ॥ 1 ॥
   evaṁ — thus; priyāvacaḥ — beloved's words; śrutvā — having heard; jñātvā — having known; tattvaṁ — essence; maheśituḥ — of the great lord; traipuram — of Tripura; cinmayam — made of consciousness; hemalekhā-vākyena — by Hemalekha's words; niścitam — determined
   Having heard the beloved’s words and grasped the essence of the great lord, Hemachuda understood from Hemalekha's explanation that Tripura is composed of consciousness.
   
   Verse 2
   आश्वस्तचित्तस्त्रिपुरां गुणरूपां महेश्वरीम्‌ ।
   ज्ञात्वा गुरुभ्यः परमां माहैश्वर्यविभावितः ॥ २ ॥
   āśvastacittas tripurāṁ guṇarūpāṁ maheśvarīm ।
   jñātvā gurubhyaḥ paramāṁ māhaiśvaryavibhāvitaḥ ॥ 2 ॥
   āśvastacittas — with a calmed mind; tripurām — Tripura; guṇarūpām — having qualities; maheśvarīm — the great goddess; jñātvā — having known; gurubhyaḥ — from the teachers; paramām — supreme; māhaiśvaryavibhāvitaḥ — endowed with supreme powers
   With a calm mind, having learned from the teachers about Tripura, the great goddess endowed with supreme powers, he recognized her supreme qualities.
   
   Verse 3
   तामेकभावानुगतो हेमचूडोऽभवद्‌ दृढम्‌ ।
   एवं परोपासनेन व्यतीयुः केऽपि मासकाः ॥ ३ ॥
   tām ekabhāvānugato hemacūḍo'bhavad dṛḍham ।
   evaṁ paropāsanena vyatīyuḥ ke'pi māsakāḥ ॥ 3 ॥
   tām — her; eka-bhāva-anugataḥ — following single-mindedly; hemacūḍaḥ — Hemachuda; abhavad — became; dṛḍham — firmly; evaṁ — thus; paropāsanena — by worshiping; vyatīyuḥ — passed; ke'pi — some; māsakāḥ — months
   Single-mindedly devoted to her, Hemachuda worshipped her with unwavering dedication, and thus, several months passed.
   
   Verse 4
   त्रिपुरा परमेशानी प्रसादमकरोद्‌ हृदि ।
   विषयाद्विमुखं चित्तं विचारपरमं बभौ ॥ ४ ॥
   tripurā parameśānī prasādamakarod hṛdi ।
   viṣayādvimukhaṁ cittaṁ vicāraparamaṁ babhau ॥ 4 ॥
   tripurā — Tripura; parameśānī — the supreme goddess; prasādam — grace; akarot — bestowed; hṛdi — in the heart; viṣayāt — from objects; vimukhaṁ — turned away; cittaṁ — mind; vicāra-paramaṁ — deeply contemplative; babhau — became
   The supreme goddess Tripura graced his heart, turning his mind away from worldly objects and leading him into deep contemplation.
   
   Verse 5
   एतावद्‌ दुर्लभं लोके परानुग्रहमन्तरा ।
   विचारप्रवणं चित्तं यन्मुख्यं मोक्षकारणम्‌ ॥ ५ ॥
   etāvad durlabhaṁ loke parānugrahamantarā ।
   vicāra-pravaṇaṁ cittaṁ yanmukhyaṁ mokṣakāraṇam ॥ 5 ॥
   etāvat — this much; durlabhaṁ — rare; loke — in the world; parānugraham — other's grace; antarā — without; vicāra-pravaṇam — inclined to contemplation; cittam — mind; yat — which; mukhyam — principal; mokṣa-kāraṇam — cause of liberation
   Such a mind inclined toward contemplation, which is the principal cause of liberation, is rare in the world without the grace of others.
   
   Verse 6
   राम यावन्न जायेत विचारपरमं मनः ।
   न तावच्छ्रेयसा योग उपायानां शतैः क्वचित्‌ ॥ ६ ॥
   rāma yāvanna jāyeta vicāraparamaṁ manaḥ ।
   na tāvacchreyasā yoga upāyānāṁ śataiḥ kvacit ॥ 6 ॥
   rāma — O Rama; yāvat — until; na — not; jāyeta — is born; vicāra-paramaṁ — deeply contemplative; manaḥ — mind; na — not; tāvat — then; śreyasā — with the ultimate good; yoga — union; upāyānāṁ — of means; śataiḥ — by hundreds; kvacit — anywhere
   O Rama, until a deeply contemplative mind arises, the ultimate good cannot be attained by any number of means.
   
   Verse 7
   अथ भूयः स कस्मिंश्चिद्दिने रहसि वै तया ।
   सङ्गतः प्रिययाऽत्यन्तविचारपरमानसः ॥ ७ ॥
   atha bhūyaḥ sa kasmiṁścid dine rahasi vai tayā ।
   saṅgataḥ priyayā'tyantavicāraparamānasaḥ ॥ 7 ॥
   atha — then; bhūyaḥ — again; saḥ — he; kasmiṁścit — on some; dine — day; rahasi — in private; vai — indeed; tayā — with her; saṅgataḥ — together; priyayā — with the beloved; atyanta-vicāra-paramānasaḥ — with a deeply contemplative mind
   Then, on another day, he was alone with his beloved, with a deeply contemplative mind.
   
   Verse 8
   आयान्तं स्वनिकेतं तं दूरात्‌ कान्तं ददर्श सा ।
   उत्थाय तं समानीय स्वासने विनिवेश्य च ॥ ८ ॥
   āyāntaṁ svaniketaṁ taṁ dūrāt kāntaṁ dadarśa sā ।
   utthāya taṁ samānīya svāsane viniveśya ca ॥ 8 ॥
   āyāntaṁ — coming; svaniketam — to his place; tam — him; dūrāt — from a distance; kāntam — beloved; dadarśa — saw; sā — she; utthāya — rising; tam — him; samānīya — bringing; svāsane — on her seat; viniveśya — seating; ca — and
   Seeing him approach from a distance, she rose, welcomed him in, and seated him on her seat.
   
   Verse 9
   पादप्रक्षालनाद्दैस्तं पूजयित्वा यथाविधि ।
   प्रोवाचामृतनिष्यन्दसुन्दरं परमं वचः ॥ ९ ॥
   pāda-prakṣālanād daiṣṭaṁ pūjayitvā yathāvidhi ।
   provācāmṛta-niṣyanda-sundaraṁ paramaṁ vacaḥ ॥ 9 ॥
   pāda-prakṣālanāt — by washing the feet; daiṣṭam — with respect; pūjayitvā — having worshipped; yathāvidhi — according to the rule; provāca — spoke; amṛta-niṣyanda-sundaram — beautiful with the flow of nectar; paramam — supreme; vacaḥ — words
   After washing his feet with reverence and worshiping him according to tradition, she spoke supreme words, flowing with the beauty of nectar.
   
   Verse 10
   प्रेष्ठ ! त्वामद्य पश्यामि चिराय ननु ते वपुः ।
   नीरुजं कच्चिदासीद्वै यतो रोगास्पदं वपुः ॥ १० ॥
   preṣṭha! tvām adya paśyāmi cirāya nanu te vapuḥ ।
   nīrujaṁ kaccid āsīd vai yato rogāspadaṁ vapuḥ ॥ 10 ॥
   preṣṭha — beloved; tvām — you; adya — today; paśyāmi — I see; cirāya — after a long time; nanu — indeed; te — your; vapuḥ — body; nīrujam — free from disease; kaccid — whether; āsīt — has been; vai — indeed; yataḥ — since; roga-āspadam — disease-prone; vapuḥ — body
   Beloved, today I see you after a long time. Is your body free from illness, or was it troubled by disease?
   
   Verse 11
   तन्ममाचक्ष्व वृत्तान्तं यतो नाहं स्मृता त्वया ।
   ननु मामसमालोक्य चाप्रभाष्य कदापि ते ॥ ११ ॥
   tan mama ācakṣva vṛttāntaṁ yato nāhaṁ smṛtā tvayā ।
   nanu mām asamālokya cāprabhāṣya kadāpi te ॥ 11 ॥
   tat — that; mama — to me; ācakṣva — tell; vṛttāntam — the events; yataḥ — since; na — not; aham — I; smṛtā — remembered; tvayā — by you; nanu — indeed; mām — me; asamālokya — without seeing; ca — and; aprabhāṣya — without speaking; kadāpi — even; te — your
   Please tell me what has happened, as you did not remember me or speak to me during this time.
   
   Verse 12
   नात्यगाद्दिनभागोऽपि तदेवं कुत आस्थितम्‌ ।
   मन्येऽहं तेऽनभिमते वर्तनं नहि वर्त्मनि ॥ १२ ॥
   nātyagād dina-bhāgo'pi tad evaṁ kuta āsthitam ।
   manye'haṁ te'nabhimate vartanaṁ nahi vartmani ॥ 12 ॥
   na — not; atyagāt — passed; dina-bhāgaḥ — part of the day; api — even; tat — that; evaṁ — thus; kutaḥ — how; āsthitam — happened; manye — I think; ahaṁ — I; te — your; anabhimate — in displeasure; vartanam — existence; nahi — not; vartmani — on the path
   Not even a part of the day went by like this before. How did this happen? I fear you might be displeased with me and not following the right path.
   
   Verse 13
   स्वप्ने वापि कुतोऽन्यत्र कुत एवमभूद्‌ वद ।
   कथं रात्रिस्त्वया नीता चैकापि युगसम्मिता ॥ १३ ॥
   svapne vāpi kuto'nyatra kuta evam abhūd vada ।
   kathaṁ rātriḥ tvayā nītā caikāpi yuga-sammatā ॥ 13 ॥
   svapne — in a dream; vā — or; api — even; kutaḥ — where; anyatra — elsewhere; kutaḥ — how; evam — thus; abhūt — happened; vada — tell; kathaṁ — how; rātriḥ — night; tvayā — by you; nītā — spent; ca — and; ekā — one; api — even; yuga-sammatā — like an age
   How did this happen, even in a dream or elsewhere? Tell me, how did you spend a night that once felt like an age?
   
   Verse 14
   मां विना प्राक्‌ क्षणोऽप्येको युगकल्पः सुदुःसहः ।
   इत्युक्त्वा सा समाश्लिष्य खिन्नेवाभूत्क्षणं ततः ॥ १४ ॥
   māṁ vinā prāk kṣaṇo'pyeko yuga-kalpaḥ suduḥsahaḥ ।
   ity uktvā sā samāśliṣya khinnevābhūt kṣaṇaṁ tataḥ ॥ 14 ॥
   māṁ vinā — without me; prāk — before; kṣaṇaḥ — moment; api — even; ekaḥ — one; yuga-kalpaḥ — like an age; suduḥsahaḥ — very hard to bear; iti uktvā — having said thus; sā — she; samāśliṣya — embracing; khinnā iva abhūt — appeared distressed; kṣaṇam — for a moment; tataḥ — then
   Without me, even a single moment felt like an age, unbearably long. Saying this, she embraced him and appeared briefly distressed.
   
   Verse 15
   सोऽपि प्रियासमाश्लिष्टो नेषद्विकृतिमाययौ ।
   प्राह प्रिये न मामेवं विमोहयितुमर्हसि ॥ १५ ॥
   so'pi priyāsamāliṣṭo neṣadvikṛtim āyayau ।
   prāha priye na māmevaṁ vimohayitum arhasi ॥ 15 ॥
   saḥ api — he also; priyā-samāliṣṭaḥ — embraced by the beloved; neṣat — slight; vikṛtim — distortion; āyayau — occurred; prāha — said; priye — dear; na — not; mām — me; evaṁ — thus; vimohayitum — to confuse; arhasi — you should
   He also embraced his beloved and showed no sign of discomfort. He said, "Dear, you should not confuse me like this."
   
   Verse 16
   ज्ञाता मयाऽसि सुद्रुदं नास्ति ते शोककारणम्‌ ।
   परावरज्ञा त्वं धीरा मोहस्त्वां वै कथं स्पृशेत्‌ ॥ १६ ॥
   jñātā mayā'si sudṛḍhaṁ nāsti te śoka-kāraṇam ।
   parāvara-jñā tvaṁ dhīrā mohastvāṁ vai kathaṁ spṛśet ॥ 16 ॥
   jñātā — known; mayā — by me; asi — you are; sudṛḍhaṁ — firmly; nāsti — there is not; te — for you; śoka-kāraṇam — cause of sorrow; parāvara-jñā — knower of the ultimate; tvam — you; dhīrā — wise; mohaḥ — delusion; tvām — you; vai — indeed; katham — how; spṛśet — could touch
   I know you well; there is no reason for sorrow for you. How could delusion touch you, wise one who knows the ultimate truth?
   
   Verse 17
   तत्त्वां प्रष्टुं समायातो यत्तद्वक्ष्यामि संशृणु ।
   यत्‌ प्राक्‌ स्ववृत्तं कथितं तत्‌ स्फुटं मे समीरय ॥ १७ ॥
   tattvāṁ praṣṭuṁ samāyāto yat tad vakṣyāmi saṁśṛṇu ।
   yat prāk svavṛttaṁ kathitaṁ tat sphuṭaṁ me samīraya ॥ 17 ॥
   tattvāṁ — truly; praṣṭum — to ask; samāyātaḥ — come; yat — that; tad — it; vakṣyāmi — I will say; saṁśṛṇu — listen; yat — which; prāk — before; svavṛttam — own events; kathitam — spoken; tat — that; sphuṭam — clearly; me — to me; samīraya — tell
   I have come to truly ask you something; listen to what I will say. Tell me clearly about the events you mentioned before.
   
   Verse 18
   का सा ते जननी प्रोक्ता सखी वा तत्पतिश्च कः ।
   तत्पुत्राद्या अपि च के मम वा ते क्व संवद ॥ १८ ॥
   kā sā te jananī proktā sakhī vā tat-patiś ca kaḥ ।
   tat-putrādyā api ca ke mama vā te kva saṁvada ॥ 18 ॥
   kā — who; sā — she; te — your; jananī — mother; proktā — said; sakhī — friend; vā — or; tat-patiḥ — her husband; ca — and; kaḥ — who; tat-putrādyāḥ — her children; api ca — and also; ke — who; mama — my; vā — or; te — yours; kva — where; saṁvada — they
   Who is the mother you mentioned, who is your friend, and who is her husband? Who are her children, and are they yours or mine? Where are they?
   
   Verse 19
   न तन्मया सुविदितं न तन्मन्ये मृषोदितम्‌ ।
   किन्तु त्वया निगदितं व्यपदेशेन सर्वथा ॥ १९ ॥
   na tan mayā suviditaṁ na tan manye mṛṣoditam ।
   kintu tvayā nigaditaṁ vyapadeśena sarvathā ॥ 19 ॥
   na — not; tat — that; mayā — by me; suviditam — well known; na — not; tat — that; manye — I think; mṛṣā-uditam — falsely spoken; kintu — but; tvayā — by you; nigaditam — spoken; vyapadeśena — by implication; sarvathā — completely
   I do not know that well, and I don't think it's spoken falsely. However, it seems that you are implying something with what you've said.
   
   Verse 20
   तद्विविच्य प्रकथय यथा ज्ञास्ये त्वहं स्फुटम्‌ ।
   अहं त्वां सुप्रपन्नोऽस्मि छिन्धि मे हृदि संशयम्‌ ॥ २० ॥
   tad vivicya prakathaya yathā jñāsye tvahaṁ sphuṭam ।
   ahaṁ tvāṁ suprapanno'smi chindhi me hṛdi saṁśayam ॥ 20 ॥
   tat — that; vivicya — analyzing; prakathaya — explain; yathā — so that; jñāsye — I will know; tvam — you; ahaṁ — I; sphuṭam — clearly; ahaṁ — I; tvām — you; suprapannaḥ — devoted; asmi — am; chindhi — remove; me — my; hṛdi — in the heart; saṁśayam — doubt
   Please analyze and explain that to me clearly. I am devoted to you, and I need you to remove the doubt from my heart.
   
   Verse 21
   एवमुक्ता हेमलेखा प्रसन्नवदनेक्षणा ।
   मत्वा सुनिर्मलधियं परानुग्रहसंयुतम्‌ ॥ २१ ॥
   evam uktā hemalekhā prasanna-vadanekṣaṇā ।
   matvā sunirmala-dhiyaṁ parānugraha-saṁyutam ॥ 21 ॥
   evam — thus; uktā — addressed; hemalekhā — Hemalekha; prasanna — clear; vadana — face; īkṣaṇā — eyes; matvā — thinking; sunirmala — pure; dhiyaṁ — mind; para-anugraha — divine grace; saṁyutam — endowed with
   Thus addressed, Hemalekha, with clear eyes and a pure mind, reflected on the divine grace bestowed on him.
   
   Verse 22
   नूनमेषोऽतिविमुखो विषयेभ्योऽतिधैर्यतः ।
   विद्धः शक्त्या महेशान्यां फलितः पुण्यसञ्चयः ॥ २२ ॥
   nūnam eṣo'ti-vimukho viṣayebhyo'ti-dhairyataḥ ।
   viddhaḥ śaktyā maheśānyāṁ phalitaḥ puṇya-saṁcayaḥ ॥ 22 ॥
   nūnam — indeed; eṣaḥ — he; ati-vimukhaḥ — very detached; viṣayebhyaḥ — from sense objects; ati-dhairyataḥ — due to great fortitude; viddhaḥ — struck; śaktyā — by the power; maheśānyām — of Lord Mahesha; phalitaḥ — fruitful; puṇya-saṁcayaḥ — accumulation of merit
   Indeed, he is highly detached from sense objects due to his great fortitude, influenced by the power of Lord Mahesha and enriched by the accumulation of merit.
   
   Verse 23
   कालः प्रबोधने चायं बोधयामि ततस्त्विमम्‌ ।
   नाथ तेऽहो महाभाग्यं प्राप्तमीशकृपावशात्‌ ॥ २३ ॥
   kālaḥ prabodhane cāyaṁ bodhayāmi tatas tvimam ।
   nātha te'aho mahābhāgyaṁ prāptam īśakṛpāvaśāt ॥ 23 ॥
   kālaḥ — time; prabodhane — for awakening; ca — and; ayam — this; bodhayāmi — I will enlighten; tataḥ — therefore; imam — him; nātha — O lord; te — your; aho — indeed; mahābhāgyam — great fortune; prāptam — obtained; īśa-kṛpā-vaśāt — due to the grace of the Lord
   It is time for awakening, and so I will enlighten him. O Lord, your great fortune has indeed come through the grace of the Lord.
   
   Verse 24
   अन्यथा नैव विषयवैरस्यं पश्यति क्वचित्‌ ।
   एतल्लक्षणमीशस्यानुग्रहे ज्ञेयमादितः ॥ २४ ॥
   anyathā naiva viṣaya-vairasyaṁ paśyati kvacit ।
   etallakṣaṇam īśasya anugrahe jñeyam āditaḥ ॥ 24 ॥
   anyathā — otherwise; na — not; eva — indeed; viṣaya-vairasyam — disinterest in sense objects; paśyati — sees; kvacit — anywhere; etat-lakṣaṇam — this characteristic; īśasya — of the Lord; anugrahe — in grace; jñeyam — to be known; āditaḥ — from the beginning
   Otherwise, disinterest in sense objects is not commonly observed. This trait is recognized from the beginning as the grace of the Lord.
   
   Verse 25
   भोगवैरस्यमपरं विचारप्रवणं मनः ।
   हन्त ते सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि वृत्तिं प्रोक्तां सदात्मनः ॥ २५ ॥
   bhoga-vairasyam-aparaṁ vicāra-pravaṇaṁ manaḥ ।
   hanta te sampravakṣyāmi vṛttiṁ proktāṁ sadātmanāḥ ॥ 25 ॥
   bhoga-vairasyam — disinterest in enjoyment; aparam — another; vicāra-pravaṇam — inclined to contemplation; manaḥ — mind; hanta — behold; te — to you; sampravakṣyāmi — I will explain; vṛttim — conduct; proktam — stated; sadātmanāḥ — by the wise
   Behold, I will explain to you the conduct stated by the wise, the mind's disinterest in enjoyment and inclination towards contemplation.
   
   Verse 26
   परा चितिर्मे जननी सखी बुद्धिर्मता मम ।
   अविद्या त्वसती सोक्ता यया बुद्धिः सुसङ्गता ॥ २६ ॥
   parā citir me jananī sakhī buddhir matā mama ।
   avidyā tv asatī sŏktā yayā buddhiḥ su-saṅgatā ॥ 26 ॥
   parā — supreme; citiḥ — consciousness; me — my; jananī — mother; sakhī — friend; buddhiḥ — intellect; matā — considered; mama — by me; avidyā — ignorance; tu — indeed; asatī — unreal; sŏktā — is called; yayā — by which; buddhiḥ — intellect; su-saṅgatā — well-associated
   The supreme consciousness is my mother; intellect is regarded as my friend, and ignorance, which is her husband, is considered unreal. It is through this ignorance that the intellect is well-associated.
   
   Verse 27
   अविद्यायास्तु सामर्थ्य लोके स्पष्टं विचित्रितम्‌ ।
   यद्रज्जौ सर्पमाभास्य महाभीतिं प्रयच्छति ॥ २७ ॥
   avidyāyās tu sāmarthya loke spaṣṭaṁ vicitritam ।
   yad rajjau sarpam ābhāsya mahābhītiṁ prayacchati ॥ 27 ॥
   avidyāyāḥ — of ignorance; tu — indeed; sāmarthya — power; loke — in the world; spaṣṭam — clearly; vicitritam — seen; yat — that; rajjau — in the rope; sarpam — snake; ābhāsya — appearing; mahā-bhītim — great fear; prayacchati — causes
   The power of ignorance is evident in the world, as it makes a rope appear like a snake and instills great fear.
   
   Verse 28
   महामोहस्तु तत्पुत्रो मनस्तस्य सुतोऽभवत्‌ ।
   तस्य पत्नी कल्पना स्यात्तत्सुताः पञ्च येऽभवन्‌ ॥ २८ ॥
   mahāmohas tu tatputro manas tasya suto'bhavat ।
   tasya patnī kalpanā syāt tat-sutāḥ pañca ye'bhavan ॥ 28 ॥
   mahāmohaḥ — great delusion; tu — indeed; tat-putraḥ — its son; manaḥ — mind; tasya — its; sutaḥ — son; abhavat — was; tasya — its; patnī — wife; kalpanā — imagination; syāt — is; tat-sutāḥ — their sons; pañca — five; ye — who; abhavan — were
   The great delusion, the mind, is its offspring and their child, imagination is its spouse, and the sensory organs are its five sons.
   
   Verse 29
   ज्ञानेन्द्रियाणि ते पञ्च तत्स्थानं गोलकं भवेत्‌ ।
   विषयाणां प्रमोषस्तु संस्कारो मनसो भवेत्‌ ॥ २९ ॥
   jñānendriyāṇi te pañca tat sthānaṁ golakaṁ bhavet ।
   viṣayāṇāṁ pramoṣas tu saṁskāro manaso bhavet ॥ 29 ॥
   jñānendriyāṇi — sensory organs; te — they; pañca — five; tat — their; sthānam — place; golakam — sphere; bhavet — is; viṣayāṇām — of objects; pramoṣaḥ — perception; tu — indeed; saṁskāraḥ — impression; manasaḥ — of the mind; bhavet — is
   The five sensory organs are their domain, and the perception of objects is the impression left on the mind.
   
   Verse 30
   तद्भोगः स्वप्नभोगः स्यात्‌ कल्पनायाः स्वसा तु या ।
   महाशना भवेदाशा तस्या यौ तनुजावुभौ ॥ ३० ॥
   tad bhogaḥ svapnabhogaḥ syāt kalpanāyāḥ svasā tu yā ।
   mahāśanā bhaved āśā tasyā yau tanujāvubhau ॥ 30 ॥
   tad — that; bhogaḥ — enjoyment; svapnabhogaḥ — dream enjoyment; syāt — is; kalpanāyāḥ — of imagination; svasā — sister; tu — indeed; yā — who; mahāśanā — great consumer; bhavet — is; āśā — desire; tasyāḥ — her; yau — who; tanujau — sons; ubhau — both
   That enjoyment of senses is a dreamlike pleasure, like a sister of imagination. His other wife is intense desire, and her two sons are anger and greed.
   
   Verse 31
   क्रोधो लोभश्च तावुक्तौ तत्पुरं तु शरीरकम्‌ ।
   मम यस्तु महामन्त्रः स्वरूपस्फुरणं हि तत्‌ ॥ ३१ ॥
   krodho lobhaś ca tāv uktau tat-puraṁ tu śarīrakam ।
   mama yas tu mahā-mantraḥ svarūpa-sphuraṇaṁ hi tat ॥ 31 ॥
   krodhaḥ — anger; lobhaḥ — greed; ca — and; tau — they; uktau — are said; tat-puraṁ — their city; tu — indeed; śarīrakam — body; mama — my; yaḥ — which; tu — indeed; mahā-mantraḥ — great mantra; svarūpa-sphuraṇam — self-revelation; hi — indeed; tat — that
   Anger and greed are considered their city, which is the body. My great mantra is indeed the self-revelation.
   
   Verse 32
   प्राणः प्रचारः सम्प्रोक्तो मनसस्तु प्रियः सखा ।
   कान्ताराद्यास्तु नरका एवं सर्वं प्रकीर्तितम्‌ ॥ ३२ ॥
   prāṇaḥ pracāraḥ samprokto manasas tu priyaḥ sakhā ।
   kāntārādyās tu narakā evaṁ sarvaṁ prakīrtitam ॥ 32 ॥
   prāṇaḥ — breath; pracāraḥ — movement; samproktaḥ — is called; manasaḥ — of the mind; tu — indeed; priyaḥ — dear; sakhā — friend; kāntārāḥ — forests; ādyāḥ — and others; tu — indeed; narakāḥ — hells; evaṁ — thus; sarvam — everything; prakīrtitam — is described
   Breath is referred to as Pracara and is the close friend of the mind. Forests and similar places are described as hells. Thus, everything is explained.
   
   Verse 33
   मया बुद्धेः सङ्गमस्तु समाधिरभिधीयते ।
   मन्मातृलोकसंप्राप्तिर्मोक्षः प्रिय उदाहृतः ॥ ३३ ॥
   mayā buddheḥ saṅgamastu samādhir abhidhīyate ।
   man-mātṛ-loka-saṁprāptir mokṣaḥ priya udāhṛtaḥ ॥ 33 ॥
   mayā — by me; buddheḥ — of intellect; saṅgamaḥ — union; tu — indeed; samādhiḥ — concentration; abhidhīyate — is called; man-mātṛ-loka — my mother's world; saṁprāptiḥ — attainment; mokṣaḥ — liberation; priya — dear; udāhṛtaḥ — is stated
   The union of intellect with me is termed concentration. The attainment of my mother’s world is described as liberation, dear.
   
   Verse 34
   एवं प्रोक्तः स्ववृत्तान्तस्त्वमप्येवविधो ननु ।
   तद्युक्त्यैतत्‌ सुविज्ञाय परं श्रेयः समाप्नुहि ॥ ३४ ॥
   evaṁ proktaḥ sva-vṛttāntas tvam apy evavidho nanu ।
   tad yuktyaitat suvigñāya paraṁ śreyaḥ samāpnuhu ॥ 34 ॥
   evaṁ — thus; proktaḥ — described; sva-vṛttāntaḥ — own story; tvam — you; api — also; eva-vidhaḥ — similar; nanu — indeed; tat — that; yuktyā — with reasoning; etat — this; suvigñāya — understanding well; param — supreme; śreyaḥ — welfare; samāpnuhu — attain
   Thus, I have shared my own story. Your story is also similar. Understand this clearly through reasoning, attain the supreme welfare.


   
   इति श्रीमज्ज्ञानखण्डे हेमचूडोपाख्याने संसाराख्यायिकाविवरणे अष्टमोऽध्यायः ॥
   
   Thus ends the eighth chapter named "Explanation of the Description of the World" in the revered Knowledge Section in the story of Hemachuda.
   
   
   

9. HEMACHUDA’S REST
   Verse 1
   श्रुत्वेत्थं प्रियया प्रोक्तं हेमचूडोऽतिविस्मितः ।
   हर्षगद्गदया वाचा पुनर्वक्तुं प्रचक्रमे ॥ १ ॥
   śrutv-etthaṁ priyayā proktaṁ hemacūḍo'tivismitaḥ ।
   harṣa-gadgadayā vācā punar-vaktuṁ pracakrame ॥ 1 ॥
   śrutvā — having heard; itthaṁ — thus; priyayā — by the beloved; proktaṁ — spoken; hemacūḍaḥ — Hemachuda; ati-vismitaḥ — very astonished; harṣa-gadgadayā — with a voice choked with joy; vācā — in words; punaḥ — again; vaktuṁ — to speak; pracakrame — began
   Having heard his beloved’s words, Hemachuda was astonished. With a voice choked with joy, he began to speak again.
   
   Verse 2
   धन्या प्रियेऽसि निपुणा अहो ते ज्ञानवैभवम्‌ ।
   किं वर्णयामि यत्‌ प्रोक्तमाख्यारूपतयाऽखिलम्‌ ॥ २ ॥
   dhanyā priye'si nipuṇā aho te jñāna-vaibhavam ।
   kiṁ varṇayāmi yat proktam ākhyā-rūpatayā'khilam ॥ 2 ॥
   dhanyā — blessed; priye — dear; asi — you are; nipuṇā — skillful; aho — oh; te — your; jñāna-vaibhavam — splendor of knowledge; kiṁ — what; varṇayāmi — can I describe; yat — that; proktam — spoken; ākhyā-rūpatayā — in the form of a story; akhilam — entire
   Oh dear, you are blessed and skillful. How can I describe the splendor of your knowledge, who has spoken about that as a complete story?
   
   Verse 3
   एवंविधं स्ववृत्तं मे नाभवद्विदितं क्वचित्‌ ।
   त्वदुक्त्याऽहं सम्प्रति तत्‌ करामलकवत्‌ स्फुटम्‌ ॥ ३ ॥
   evaṁvidhaṁ sva-vṛttaṁ me nābhavad viditaṁ kvacit ।
   tvad-uktyā'haṁ samprati tat karāmala-kavat sphuṭam ॥ 3 ॥
   evaṁvidham — such; sva-vṛttam — own story; me — my; na abhavat — was not; viditam — known; kvacit — anywhere; tvad-uktyā — by your words; ahaṁ — I; samprati — now; tat — that; kara-amalaka-vat — like a fruit in hand; sphuṭam — clear
   I was unaware of such a story about my nature. Your words have made it as clear to me as a fruit in my hand.
   
   Verse 4
   स्मराम्यनुभवाम्यन्तरहो लोकक्रियाऽद्भुता ।
   का सा परा चितिर्माता कथं तस्यास्तु नो जनिः ॥ ४ ॥
   smarāmy anubhavāmy antar aho loka-kriyā'dbhutā ।
   kā sā parā citir mātā kathaṁ tasyāstu no janiḥ ॥ 4 ॥
   smarāmi — I remember; anubhavāmi — I experience; antar — within; aho — oh; loka-kriyā — world actions; adbhutā — wonderful; kā — who; sā — she; parā — supreme; citiḥ — consciousness; mātā — mother; kathaṁ — how; tasyāḥ — her; tu — indeed; naḥ — our; janiḥ — birth
   I recall and experience it within the wonderful actions of the world. Who is that supreme consciousness, the mother, and how are we born from her?
   
   Verse 5
   के वा वयं स्वरूपं किमस्माकं तद्‌ ब्रवीहि मे ।
   इति पृष्टा हेमलेखा रामोवाच प्रियं प्रति ॥ ५ ॥
   ke vā vayaṁ svarūpaṁ kim asmākaṁ tad bravīhi me ।
   iti pṛṣṭā hemalekhā rāmovāca priyaṁ prati ॥ 5 ॥
   ke — who; vā — indeed; vayaṁ — we; svarūpam — nature; kim — what; asmākam — our; tat — that; bravīhi — tell; me — to me; iti — thus; pṛṣṭā — asked; hemalekhā — Hemalekha; rāmaḥ — Ram; uvāca — said; priyaṁ — to the beloved; prati — towards
   "Who are we, and what is our nature? Tell me that," he asked Hemalekha. She then spoke to his beloved.
   
   Verse 6
   नाथ शृणु प्रवक्ष्यामि गूढार्थमिदमादरात्‌ ।
   विचारयात्मनो रूपं बुद्धयाऽत्यन्तविशुद्धया ॥ ६ ॥
   nātha śṛṇu pravakṣyāmi gūḍhārtham idam ādarāt ।
   vicārayātmano rūpaṁ buddhayā'tyanta-viśuddhayā ॥ 6 ॥
   nātha — lord; śṛṇu — listen; pravakṣyāmi — I will explain; gūḍhārtham — hidden meaning; idam — this; ādarāt — with respect; vicāraya — contemplate; ātmano — of self; rūpam — form; buddhayā — with intellect; atyanta-viśuddhayā — extremely pure
   Listen, my lord, I will respectfully explain this hidden meaning. Contemplate the form of the self with an extremely pure intellect.
   
   Verse 7
   न दृश्यं नापि तद्वाच्यमतो वक्ष्यामि तत्‌ कथम्‌ ।
   ज्ञाते स्वात्मस्वरूपे वै ततो ज्ञास्यसि मातरम्‌ ॥ ७ ॥
   na dṛśyaṁ nāpi tad vācyam ato vakṣyāmi tat katham ।
   jñāte svātma-svarūpe vai tato jñāsyasi mātaram ॥ 7 ॥
   na — not; dṛśyam — visible; na api — nor; tad — that; vācyam — speakable; ataḥ — therefore; vakṣyāmi — I will say; tat — that; katham — how; jñāte — knowing; sva-ātma-svarūpe — own self-form; vai — indeed; tataḥ — then; jñāsyasi — you will know; mātaram — the mother
   It is neither visible nor speakable, so how will I explain? By knowing your own true form, you will indeed come to know the mother.
   
   Verse 8
   नह्यादेशः स्वरूपेऽस्ति तत आदेष्टृवर्जितम्‌ ।
   स्वं रूपं स्वात्मना पश्य शुद्धबुद्धिसमाश्रयम्‌ ॥ ८ ॥
   nahy ādeśaḥ svarūpe'sti tata ādeṣṭṛ-varjitam ।
   svaṁ rūpaṁ svātmanā paśya śuddha-buddhi-samāśrayam॥ 8 ॥
   na hi — indeed not; ādeśaḥ — order; svarūpe — in form; asti — is; tataḥ — therefore; ādeṣṭṛ-varjitam — without a commander; svaṁ — own; rūpam — form; svātmanā — with self; paśya — see; śuddha-buddhi-samāśrayam — with pure intellect
   Indeed, there is no command in one’s true form, hence it is without a commander. Perceive your own form with your self and pure intellect.
   
   Verse 9
   देवादितिर्यगन्तानां भान्तं भानैरभासितम्‌ ।
   भान्तं सर्वत्र सर्वस्य सर्वदा मानवर्जितम्‌ ॥ ९ ॥
   devād-tiryag-antānāṁ bhāntaṁ bhānaiḥ abhāsitam ।
   bhāntaṁ sarvatra sarvasya sarvadā mānavarjitam ॥ 9 ॥
   devād — from gods; tiryag-antānām — to lower beings; bhāntam — shining; bhānaiḥ — by rays; abhāsitam — illuminated; bhāntam — shining; sarvatra — everywhere; sarvasya — of everything; sarvadā — always; mānavarjitam — without mind
   Shining from gods to lower beings, illuminated by rays, it shines everywhere, encompassing everything, always without a mind.
   
   Verse 10
   कथं कुत्र कदा केन निरूप्येतापि लेशतः ।
   मन्नेत्रं दर्शयेत्येवमुक्तमेतत्‌ प्रियाधुना ॥ १० ॥
   kathaṁ kutra kadā kena nirūpyeta api leśataḥ ।
   man-netraṁ darśayety evam uktam etat priyādhunā ॥ 10 ॥
   kathaṁ — how; kutra — where; kadā — when; kena — by whom; nirūpyeta — can be described; api — even; leśataḥ — partially; mat-netram — my eyes; darśaya — show; iti — thus; evam — so; uktam — said; etat — this; priyā-adhunā — beloved, now
   How, where, when, and by whom can it be described even partially? Now, It is similar to you asking, “Show me my eyes, beloved”.
   
   Verse 11
   नात्राचार्यस्योपयोगो यथा नयनदर्शने ।
   निपुणोऽपि महाचार्यः कथं नेत्रं प्रदर्शयेत्‌ ॥ ११ ॥
   nātrācāryasy-opayogo yathā nayana-darśane ।
   nipuṇo'pi mahācāryaḥ kathaṁ netraṁ pradarśayet ॥ 11 ॥
   na atra — not here; ācāryasya — of a teacher; upayogaḥ — use; yathā — as; nayana-darśane — in seeing eyes; nipuṇaḥ api — even skilled; mahācāryaḥ — great teacher; kathaṁ — how; netram — eyes; pradarśayet — can show
   Here, a teacher is of no use as in seeing one’s own eyes. Even a skilled great teacher, how can he show you your eyes?
   
   Verse 12
   अतो गुरुरुपायोऽत्र तदुपायप्रदर्शनात्‌ ।
   तत्ते वक्ष्याम्युपायं तच्छृणु संयतमानसः ॥ १२ ॥
   ato gurur upāyo'tra tad-upāya-pradarśanāt ।
   tat-te vakṣyāmy upāyaṁ tac-chṛṇu saṁyata-mānasaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
   ataḥ — therefore; guruḥ — teacher; upāyaḥ — means; atra — here; tat-upāya — that means; pradarśanāt — by showing; tat-te — that to you; vakṣyāmi — I will tell; upāyam — means; tat — that; śṛṇu — listen; saṁyata-mānasaḥ — with restrained mind
   Therefore, the teacher is merely a means to reveal it. I will tell you that method; listen with a restrained mind.
   
   Verse 13
   यावत्‌ त्वमात्मनि ममेत्येवं तु प्रतिपश्यसि ।
   ततः परं निजं रूपं यन्ममेति न भाति ते ॥ १३ ॥
   yāvat tvam ātmani mamety evaṁ tu pratipaśyasi ।
   tataḥ paraṁ nijaṁ rūpaṁ yan mameti na bhāti te ॥ 13 ॥
   yāvat — as long as; tvam — you; ātmani — in self; mama — mine; iti — thus; evam — so; tu — indeed; pratipaśyasi — you see; tataḥ — then; param — beyond; nijaṁ rūpam — own form; yat — which; mama — mine; iti — thus; na bhāti — does not shine; te — to you
   As long as you see "mine" in the self, your true form, which is beyond "mine," will not shine for you.
   
   Verse 14
   गत्वैकान्ते विविच्यैतद्यद्यद्‌ भाति ममत्वतः ।
   तत्तत्‌ परित्यज्य परं स्वात्मानमभिलक्षय ॥ १४ ॥
   gatv-aikānte vivicyaitad yadyad bhāti mamatvataḥ ।
   tat-tat parityajya paraṁ svātmānam abhilaḳṣaya ॥ 14 ॥
   gatvā — going; ekānte — in solitude; vivicya — discerning; etad — this; yat yat — whatever; bhāti — shines; mamatvataḥ — as mine; tat tat — that; parityajya — abandoning; param — beyond; svātmānam — self; abhilaḳṣaya — observe
   Seek solitude and discern this: whatever shines as "mine," abandon it. Beyond that, observe the self.
   
   Verse 15
   यथाहं ते ममत्वेन भासनान्नात्मता मयि ।
   सम्बन्धमात्रादात्मीया न स्वरूपगता ह्यहम्‌ ॥ १५ ॥
   yathāhaṁ te mamatvena bhāsanān nātmatā mayi ।
   sambandhamātrād ātmīyā na svarūpagatā hy aham ॥ 15 ॥
   yathā — as; ahaṁ — I; te — to you; mamatvena — as mine; bhāsanāt — shining; na — not; ātmatā — self-ness; mayi — in me; sambandha-mātrāt — by mere relation; ātmīyā — own; na — not; svarūpa-gatā — in essence; hi — indeed; aham — I
   As I appear to you as "mine," it is not because I possess self-ness. It is merely due to our relationship and your own thinking, not because of my true essence.
   
   Verse 16
   ममार्थमखिलं त्यक्त्वा यत्त्यक्तुं नैव शक्यते ।
   तमात्मानं समालक्ष्य परं श्रेयः समाप्नुहि ॥ १६ ॥
   mamārtham akhilaṁ tyaktvā yat tyaktuṁ naiva śakyate ।
   tam ātmānaṁ samālakṣya paraṁ śreyaḥ samāpnuhu ॥ 16 ॥
   mama-artham — for my sake; akhilam — all; tyaktvā — abandoning; yat — which; tyaktum — to abandon; na eva — not indeed; śakyate — is possible; tam — that; ātmānam — self; samālakṣya — realizing; param — supreme; śreyaḥ — welfare; samāpnuhu — attain
   Abandon everything for my sake, even that which cannot truly be abandoned. Realize the self and attain supreme welfare.
   
   Verse 17
   इत्युक्तः प्रियया हेमचूड उत्थाय वै द्रुतम्‌ ।
   ययावश्वं समारुह्य तत्क्षणे नगराद्‌ बहिः ॥ १७ ॥
   ity uktaḥ priyayā hemacūḍa utthāya vai drutam ।
   yayāv aśvaṁ samāruhya tatkṣaṇe nagarād bahiḥ ॥ 17 ॥
   iti — thus; uktaḥ — spoken; priyayā — by the beloved; hemacūḍaḥ — Hemachuda; utthāya — standing; vai — indeed; drutam — quickly; yayau — went; aśvam — horse; samāruhya — mounting; tat-kṣaṇe — at that moment; nagarāt — from the city; bahiḥ — out
   Thus spoken by his beloved, Hemachuda quickly stood, mounted a horse, and left the city at that moment.
   
   Verse 18
   उद्यानं नन्दनसमं प्रविश्य क्षणमात्रतः ।
   वनान्तः सौधमुन्नम्रं स्फाटिकं प्रविवेश ह ॥ १८ ॥
   udyānaṁ nandan-samaṁ praviśya kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ ।
   vanāntaḥ saudham unnamraṁ sphāṭikaṁ praviveśa ha ॥ 18 ॥
   udyānam — garden; nandan-samam — like Nandan; praviśya — entering; kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ — for a moment; vanāntaḥ — forest-end; saudham — mansion; unnamram — tall; sphāṭikam — crystal; praviveśa — entered; ha — indeed
   Entering the garden resembling Nandan in a moment, he entered a tall crystal mansion at the forest's edge.
   
   Verse 19
   विसृज्यानुचरान्‌ सर्वान्‌ द्वारपालानशासयत्‌ ।
   न कोऽप्यत्र प्रविशतु मय्येकान्तविचारणे ॥ १९ ॥
   visṛjyānucarān sarvān dvārapālān aśāsayat ।
   na ko'py atra praviśatu mayy ekānta-vicāraṇe ॥ 19 ॥
   visṛjya — dismissing; anucarān — attendants; sarvān — all; dvāra-pālān — gatekeepers; aśāsayat — ordered; na kaḥ api — no one; atra — here; praviśatu — should enter; mayi — in my; ekānta-vicāraṇe — solitary contemplation
   Dismissing all attendants and instructing the gatekeepers, he ordered that no one should enter during his solitary contemplation.
   
   Verse 20
   राजामात्याश्च गुरवो राजा वाऽप्यत्र सङ्गतः ।
   अप्रवेश्या एव यावदहमाज्ञां दिशामि वः ॥ २० ॥
   rājāmātyāś ca guravo rājā vā'py atra saṅgataḥ ।
   appraveśyā eva yāvad aham ājñāṁ diśāmi vaḥ ॥ 20 ॥
   rāja-amātyāḥ — king's ministers; ca — and; guravaḥ — teachers; rājā — king; vā — or; api — also; atra — here; saṅgataḥ — assembled; apraveśyāḥ — not allowed to enter; eva — indeed; yāvat — until; aham — I; ājñām — order; diśāmi — give; vaḥ — to you
   The king's ministers, teachers, or the king himself, even if assembled here, are not allowed to enter until I give you the order.
   
   Verse 21
   इत्युक्त्वारुह्य सौधाम्यं नवमीं भूमिमाविशत्‌ ।
   तत्र वातायने चित्रे सर्वलोकावलोकने ॥ २१ ॥
   ity-uktvā rūhya saudhāmyam navamīṁ bhūmim āviśat ।
   tatra vātāyane citre sarva-lokāvalokane ॥ 21 ॥
   iti — thus; uktvā — having spoken; rūhya — ascending; saudhāmyam — mansion; navamīm — ninth; bhūmim — floor; āviśat — entered; tatra — there; vātāyane — window; citre — beautiful; sarva-loka-avalokane — viewing all worlds
   Having spoken thus, he ascended the mansion and entered the ninth floor, where there was a beautiful window with a view of all worlds.
   
   Verse 22
   आसने मृदुतूलाढये विवेशान्यविवर्जितः ।
   मनः समाधाय दृढं विचारमकरोत्तदा ॥ २२ ॥
   āsane mṛdu-tūlāḍhye viveśānya-vivarjitaḥ ।
   manaḥ samādhāya dṛḍhaṁ vicāram akarot tadā ॥ 22 ॥
   āsane — on a seat; mṛdu-tūlāḍhye — soft and cushioned; viveśa — entered; anya-vivarjitaḥ — free from others; manaḥ — mind; samādhāya — concentrating; dṛḍham — firmly; vicāram — contemplation; akarot — did; tadā — then
   He sat on a soft cushioned seat, free from others, and then, focusing his mind firmly, he engaged in contemplation.
   
   Verse 23
   नूनमेते जनाः सर्वे कथमेवं विमोहिताः ।
   नैकोऽप्यत्र विजानाति स्वात्मानं लेशतोऽपि वै ॥ २३ ॥
   nūnam ete janāḥ sarve katham evaṁ vimohitāḥ ।
   naiko'py atra vijānāti svātmānaṁ leśato'pi vai ॥ 23 ॥
   nūnam — surely; ete — these; janāḥ — people; sarve — all; katham — how; evam — thus; vimohitāḥ — deluded; na — not; ekaḥ api — even one; atra — here; vijānāti — knows; svātmānam — own self; leśataḥ api — even slightly; vai — indeed
   How are all these people so deluded? Not even one among them knows their own self even slightly.
   
   Verse 24
   सर्वोऽपि स्वात्मनो हेतोः करोति विविधाः क्रियाः ।
   केचित्‌ पठन्ति शास्त्राणि साम्नायाङ्गानि नित्यशः ॥ २४ ॥
   sarvo'pi svātmano hetoḥ karoti vividhāḥ kriyāḥ ।
   kecit paṭhanti śāstrāṇi sāmnāyāṅgāni nityaśaḥ ॥ 24 ॥
   sarvaḥ api — all; svātmanaḥ hetoḥ — for their own self; karoti — do; vividhāḥ — various; kriyāḥ — activities; kecit — some; paṭhanti — read; śāstrāṇi — scriptures; sāmnāyāṅgāni — Vedic texts; nityaśaḥ — daily
   Everyone engages in various activities for their own sake. Some read scriptures and Vedic texts daily.
   
   Verse 25
   केचिद्धनान्यर्जयन्ति केचिच्छासति चावनिम्‌ ।
   अन्ये युध्यन्ति रिपुभिरन्ये भोगैकलम्पटाः ॥ २५ ॥
   kecid dhanāny arjayanti kecic chāsati cāvanim ।
   anye yudhyanti ripubhir anye bhogaika-lampaṭāḥ ॥ 25 ॥
   kecit — some; dhanāni — wealth; arjayanti — earn; kecit — some; śāsati — rule; ca — and; avanim — the earth; anye — others; yudhyanti — fight; ripubhiḥ — with enemies; anye — others; bhoga-eka-lampaṭāḥ — indulgent in enjoyments
   Some earn wealth, some rule the earth. Others fight with enemies, while some indulge solely in pleasures.
   
   Verse 26
   कुर्वन्त्येतत्‌ स्वार्थमेते स स्वात्मा कतमो भवेत्‌ ।
   नैनं जानाति कोऽप्यत्र कुत एवमयं भ्रमः ॥ २६ ॥
   kurvanty etat svārtham ete sa svātmā katamo bhavet ।
   nainaṁ jānāti ko'py atra kuta evam ayaṁ bhramaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
   kurvanti — do; etat — this; svārtham — for self-interest; ete — these; saḥ — he; svātmā — own self; katamaḥ — which; bhavet — may be; na — not; enam — this; jānāti — knows; kaḥ api — anyone; atra — here; kutaḥ — whence; evam — thus; ayam — this; bhramaḥ — delusion
   They do all this for self-interest, but what truly is the self? No one here knows this; where, then, does this delusion come from?
   
   Verse 27
   अहो यथावदात्मानमविदित्वैव वै कृतम्‌ ।
   व्यर्थं स्वप्ने कृतमिव तदद्य विमृशामि तम्‌ ॥ २७ ॥
   aho yathāvad ātmānam aviditvaiva vai kṛtam ।
   vyarthaṁ svapne kṛtam iva tad adya vimṛśāmi tam ॥ 27 ॥
   aho — alas; yathāvat — truly; ātmānam — self; aviditvā — without knowing; eva — indeed; kṛtam — done; vyartham — in vain; svapne — in a dream; kṛtam — done; iva — like; tat — that; adya — now; vimṛśāmi — contemplate; tam — that
   Alas, without truly knowing the self, all this has been done. It is like actions performed in vain in a dream. Now, I contemplate this.
   
   Verse 28
   गृहधान्य राज्यधनयोषित्पश्वादि किञ्चन ।
   न मे स्वरूपं भवति त्वनहन्ताश्रयत्वतः ॥ २८ ॥
   gṛha-dhānya rājya-dhana-yoṣit-paśvādi kiñcana ।
   na me svarūpaṁ bhavati tv anahantā-āśrayatvataḥ ॥ 28 ॥
   gṛha-dhānya — house and grain; rājya-dhana — kingdom and wealth; yoṣit-paśu-ādi — women and cattle; kiñcana — something; na me — not my; svarūpam — essence; bhavati — is; tu — but; anahantā-āśrayatvataḥ — due to absence of "I-ness"
   House and grain, kingdom and wealth, women and cattle, and other possessions are not my essence; as they exist in the absence of the "I-ness" in them.
   
   Verse 29
   मदर्थ भूतताहेतोर्देहोऽहं स्यां हि सर्वथा ।
   नूनं क्षत्रियदायादो गौराङ्गोऽहं न संशयः ॥ २९ ॥
   madartha bhūtatā-hetor deho'haṁ syāṁ hi sarvathā ।
   nūnaṁ kṣatriya-dāyādo gaurāṅgo'haṁ na sanśayaḥ ॥ 29 ॥
   mad-artha — for my sake; bhūtatā-hetor — due to being; dehaḥ — body; ahaṁ — I; syām — should be; hi — indeed; sarvathā — in every way; nūnam — surely; kṣatriya-dāyādaḥ — Kshatriya heir; gaura-aṅgaḥ — fair-bodied; ahaṁ — I; na — not; sanśayaḥ — doubt
   For my sake, because of my existence, I should indeed be the body in every way. Surely, I am a Kshatriya heir with a fair body, no doubt.
   
   Verse 30
   अहन्तया समाक्रान्तास्तथैतेऽपि जनाः परे ।
   इति निश्चित्य दध्यौ तं देहं राजकुमारकः ॥ ३० ॥
   ahantayā samākrāntās tathā ete'pi janāḥ pare ।
   iti niścitya dadhyau taṁ dehaṁ rāja-kumārakaḥ ॥ 30 ॥
   ahantayā — with "I-ness"; samākrāntāḥ — overcome; tathā — thus; ete — these; api — also; janāḥ — people; pare — others; iti — thus; niścitya — determining; dadhyau — contemplated; tam — that; deham — body; rāja-kumārakaḥ — prince
   With "I-ness" overcome about others, and seeing others in the same way, the prince contemplated that body.
   
   Verse 31
   अथ देहस्य चात्मत्वं प्रतिषेद्धुं प्रचक्रमे ।
   अहो कथं देह एष ममतायाः समाश्रयः ॥ ३१ ॥
   atha dehasya cātmatvaṁ pratiṣeddhuṁ pracakrame ।
   aho kathaṁ deha eṣa mamatāyāḥ samāśrayaḥ ॥ 31 ॥
   atha — then; dehasya — of the body; ca — and; ātmatvam — selfhood; pratiṣeddhuṁ — to negate; pracakrame — began; aho — alas; kathaṁ — how; deha — body; eṣaḥ — this; mamata-yāḥ — of possessiveness; samāśrayaḥ — refuge
   Then he began to negate the selfhood of the body. He thought, alas, how can this body be the refuge of possessiveness?
   
   Verse 32
   रुधिरास्थ्यादिसंघातः प्रतिक्षणविकारवान्‌ ।
   मम रूपं भवेन्नूनं छिन्नमेतत्तु लक्ष्यते ॥ ३२ ॥
   rudhirāsthīādi-saṁghātaḥ prati-kṣaṇa-vikāravān ।
   mama rūpaṁ bhaven nūnaṁ chinnam etat tu lakṣyate ॥ 32 ॥
   rudhira-asthi-ādi-saṁghātaḥ — aggregate of blood, bones, etc.; prati-kṣaṇa-vikāravān — constantly changing; mama rūpam — my form; bhavet — may be; nūnam — surely; chinnam — severed; etat — this; tu — indeed; lakṣyate — is observed
   The aggregate of blood, bones, and such, constantly changing, may surely be just my form. He severed (his attachment to the body), and indeed observed.
   
   Verse 33
   काष्ठलोष्टसमत्वेन स्वप्नादौ चान्यथा स्थितः ।
   नाहं देहोऽन्य एव स्यां प्राणोऽप्येष तथाविधः ॥ ३३ ॥
   kāṣṭha-loṣṭa-samatvena svapnādau cānyathā sthitaḥ ।
   nāhaṁ deho'nya eva syāṁ prāṇo'py eṣa tathāvidhaḥ ॥ 33 ॥
   kāṣṭha-loṣṭa-samatvena — like wood or clay; svapnādau — in dreams; ca — and; anyathā — otherwise; sthitaḥ — established; na — not; ahaṁ — I; dehaḥ — body; anyaḥ — another; eva — indeed; syām — may be; prāṇaḥ — life-breath; api — also; eṣaḥ — this; tathāvidhaḥ — likewise
   Like wood or clay established in dreams (which keep changing), similarly, I am not the body; I may indeed be something else. This life-breath is also similar.
   
   Verse 34
   मनो बुद्धिश्च नाहं स्यां यत एतन्ममेरितम्‌ ।
   अतो देहादिबुद्धयन्ता दन्य एव न संशयः ॥ ३४ ॥
   mano buddhiś ca nāhaṁ syāṁ yata etan mameritam ।
   ato dehādibuddhyanta danya eva na sanśayaḥ ॥ 34 ॥
   manaḥ — mind; buddhiḥ — intellect; ca — and; na — not; ahaṁ — I; syām — may be; yataḥ — since; etat — this; mameritam — mine; ataḥ — thus; deha-ādi-buddhy-antaḥ — from body to intellect; anyaḥ — another; eva — indeed; na — not; sanśayaḥ — doubt
   I may not be the mind or intellect, since these are mine. Thus, from body to intellect, I am indeed something else, no doubt.
   
   Verse 35
   अहं कदाचिन्नास्मीति भासनाभावहेतुतः ।
   सर्वदाऽहं भासमानः स्थित एव न संशयः ॥ ३५ ॥
   ahaṁ kadācin nāsmīti bhāsanābhāva-hetutaḥ ।
   sarvadā'haṁ bhāsamānaḥ sthita eva na sanśayaḥ ॥ 35 ॥
   ahaṁ — I; kadācit — never; na asmi — am not; iti — thus; bhāsanābhāva-hetutaḥ — due to the absence of appearance; sarvadā — always; ahaṁ — I; bhāsamānaḥ — appearing; sthitaḥ — established; eva — indeed; na sanśayaḥ — no doubt
   I am never absent, even when there is no appearance of the world. I am always established as existing, no doubt.
   
   Verse 36
   भासमानस्य तु मम केन भानमिति स्फुटम्‌ ।
   नहि जानामि तत्‌ कस्मादेतन्न विदितं मया ॥ ३६ ॥
   bhāsamānasya tu mama kena bhānam iti sphuṭam ।
   nahi jānāmi tat kasmād etan na viditaṁ mayā ॥ 36 ॥
   bhāsamānasya — of the appearing; tu — but; mama — my; kena — by what; bhānam — awareness; iti — thus; sphuṭam — clearly; nahi — not; jānāmi — I know; tat — that; kasmāt — why; etat — this; na — not; viditam — known; mayā — by me
   Clearly, what is the awareness of my existence? I do not know that; why is this unknown to me?
   
   Verse 37
   घटादिकं चक्षुराद्यैर्भासते भुवि नान्यतः ।
   प्राणस्त्वचा विभात्येष मनो ज्ञानेन चोहितम्‌ ॥ ३७ ॥
   ghaṭādikaṁ cakṣur-ādyair bhāsate bhuvi nānyataḥ ।
   prāṇas-tvaca vibhāty-eṣa mano jñānena cohitam ॥ 37 ॥
   ghaṭa-ādikam — pot and so on; cakṣur-ādyaiḥ — by eyes and so on; bhāsate — appears; bhuvi — on earth; na — not; anyataḥ — otherwise; prāṇaḥ — life-breath; tvacā — by touch; vibhāti — shines; eṣaḥ — this; manaḥ — mind; jñānena — by knowledge; ca — and; uhitam — perceived
   The pot and similar objects appear through the eyes and other senses, not otherwise on earth. This life-breath is felt through touch; the mind is perceived through knowledge by intellect.
   
   Verse 38
   एवं बुद्धिः केन च मे भासनं नाविदं त्विदम्‌ ।
   अथैषां भासनादेव नात्मा भासेत मे यदि ॥ ३८ ॥
   evaṁ buddhiḥ kena ca me bhāsanaṁ nāvidaṁ tvidam ।
   athaiṣāṁ bhāsanād eva nātmā bhāseta me yadi ॥ 38 ॥
   evam — thus; buddhiḥ — intellect; kena — by what; ca — and; me — my; bhāsanam — awareness; na — not; avidam — known; tu — indeed; idam — this; atha — thus; eṣām — of these; bhāsanāt — from awareness; eva — indeed; na — not; ātmā — self; bhāseta — shines; me — to me; yadi — if
   Thus, how is it that I am not aware of my intellect? If the self does not shine, then from where does this awareness of everything come to me?
   
   Verse 39
   तर्हि नो विमृशाम्येतांस्ततो मे भासनं भवेत्‌ ।
   इति निश्चित्य मनसा जहौ मानसगोचरम्‌ ॥ ३९ ॥
   tarhi no vimṛśāmy-etāṁs tato me bhāsanaṁ bhavet ।
   iti niścitya manasā jahau mānasa-gocaram ॥ 39 ॥
   tarhi — then; no — not; vimṛśāmi — I contemplate; etān — these; tataḥ — then; me — my; bhāsanam — awareness; bhavet — will be; iti — thus; niścitya — determining; manasā — by mind; jahau — abandoned; mānasa-gocaram — mental sphere
   Then, I will not contemplate the mind and intellect; my awareness will arise. Thus deciding, he abandoned the mental sphere through his mind.
   
   Verse 40
   अथाऽपश्यदन्धकारं गाढं तत्‌ क्षणमात्रतः ।
   इदं ममात्मनो रूपमिति निश्चितमानसः ॥ ४० ॥
   atha'apayśad-andhakāraṁ gāḍhaṁ tat kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ ।
   idaṁ mamātmano rūpam iti niścitya mānasaḥ ॥ 40 ॥
   atha — then; apayśat — saw; andhakāram — darkness; gāḍham — dense; tat — that; kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ — for a moment; idam — this; mama — my; ātmanaḥ — of self; rūpam — form; iti — thus; niścitya — determining; mānasaḥ — mind
   Then, for a moment, he saw dense darkness. Determining in his mind that this is the form of his self.
   
   Verse 41
   प्रहर्ष मतुलं लेभे चाथ भूयो व्यचिन्तयत्‌ ।
   नूनं पुनः प्रपश्यामीत्येवं चित्तं रुरोध वै ॥ ४१ ॥
   praharṣa matulaṁ lebhe cātha bhūyo vyacintayat ।
   nūnaṁ punaḥ prapaśyāmītyevaṁ cittaṁ rurodha vai ॥ 41 ॥
   praharṣa — great joy; matulam — incomparable; lebhe — obtained; ca — and; atha — then; bhūyaḥ — again; vyacintayat — thought; nūnam — surely; punaḥ — again; prapaśyāmi — I will see; iti — thus; evaṁ — so; cittam — mind; rurodha — restrained; vai — indeed
   He experienced incomparable joy by doing this and then thought, "Surely, I will see again." With this in mind, he restrained his thoughts once more.
   
   Verse 42
   चञ्चलं हठयोगेन निरुद्धं समवैक्षत ।
   तेजःपुञ्जमनाद्यन्तं भास्वरं क्षणमात्रतः ॥ ४२ ॥
   cañcalaṁ haṭhayogena niruddhaṁ samavaikṣata ।
   tejaḥ-puñjam-anādyantaṁ bhāsvaraṁ kṣaṇamātrataḥ ॥ 42 ॥
   cañcalam — restless; haṭha-yogena — by forceful practice; niruddham — restrained; samavaikṣata — saw clearly; tejaḥ-puñjam — a mass of light; anādi-antam — without beginning or end; bhāsvaram — shining; kṣaṇa-mātrataḥ — for a moment
   Through forceful practice, he restrained his restless mind and clearly saw a mass of light, without beginning or end, shining for a moment.
   
   Verse 43
   प्रबुद्धश्चिन्तयामास किमेतदिति विस्मितः ।
   अहो पश्यामि विविधं किमात्मानं कथं त्विदम्‌ ॥ ४३ ॥
   prabuddhaś-cintayāmāsa kim-etad-iti vismitaḥ ।
   aho paśyāmi vividhaṁ kimātmānaṁ kathaṁ tvidam ॥ 43 ॥
   prabuddhaḥ — awakened; cintayāmāsa — thought; kim — what; etat — this; iti — thus; vismitaḥ — amazed; aho — oh; paśyāmi — I see; vividham — various; kim — what; ātmānam — self; katham — how; tu — indeed; idam — this
   Awakened, he thought, "What is this?" Amazed, he said, "Oh, I see various forms. What is this self, and how does this happen?"
   
   Verse 44
   भूयः पश्यामि चेव्येवं रुरोध स्वमनस्तदा ।
   विलीनं निद्रया चित्तं बभौ चिरतरं दृढम्‌ ॥ ४४ ॥
   bhūyaḥ paśyāmi cevy-evaṁ rurodha svamanas-tadā ।
   vilīnaṁ nidrayā cittaṁ babhau cirataraṁ dṛḍham ॥ 44 ॥
   bhūyaḥ — again; paśyāmi — I see; ca — and; evam — thus; rurodha — restrained; sva-manas — his mind; tadā — then; vilīnam — absorbed; nidrayā — by sleep; cittam — mind; babhau — appeared; cirataram — for a long time; dṛḍham — firm
   Then, he restrained his mind once more, saying, "I will see again." His mind, absorbed in sleep, remained steady for a long time.
   
   Verse 45
   तत्रापश्यत्‌ स्वप्नजालं विचित्रानेकदर्शनम्‌ ।
   अथ प्रबुद्धोऽत्यन्तं वै चिन्तां प्राप महत्तराम्‌ ॥ ४५ ॥
   tatrāpaśyat svapna-jālaṁ vicitrāneka-darśanam ।
   atha prabuddho'tyantaṁ vai cintāṁ prāpa mahattarām ॥ 45 ॥
   tatra — there; apaśyat — saw; svapna-jālam — a network of dreams; vicitra-aneka-darśanam — various strange visions; atha — then; prabuddhaḥ — awakened; atyantam — greatly; vai — indeed; cintām — thought; prāpa — attained; mahattarām — great
   There, he saw a network of dreams, filled with various strange visions. Then, greatly awakened, he attained profound thought.
   
   Verse 46
   किमहं निद्रयाच्छन्नः स्वप्नान्‌ समवलोकयम्‌ ।
   तमस्तेजश्चापि दृष्टमहो स्वप्नात्मकं भवेत्‌ ॥ ४६ ॥
   kim-ahaṁ nidrayācchannaḥ svapnān samavalokayām ।
   tamas-tejaś-cāpi dṛṣṭam-aho svapnātmakaṁ bhavet ॥ 46 ॥
   kim — what; aham — I; nidrayā — by sleep; ācchannaḥ — covered; svapnān — dreams; samavalokayām — saw; tamaḥ — darkness; tejaḥ — light; ca — and; api — also; dṛṣṭam — seen; aho — oh; svapna-ātmakam — of dream nature; bhavet — may be
   What dreams did I see while covered by sleep? I saw both darkness and light; perhaps the self has a dream-like nature.
   
   Verse 47
   स्वप्नस्तु मानसोल्लासस्तदेतं वर्जये कथम्‌ ।
   भूयो निगृह्य पश्यामीत्येवं निश्चित्य वै दृढम्‌ ॥ ४७ ॥
   svapnas-tu mānasollāsas-tadetaṁ varjaye katham ।
   bhūyo nigṛhya paśyāmītyevaṁ niścitya vai dṛḍham ॥ 47 ॥
   svapnaḥ — dream; tu — indeed; mānasa-ullāsaḥ — mental delight; tad — that; etam — this; varjaye — I will abandon; katham — how; bhūyaḥ — again; nigṛhya — restraining; paśyāmi — I see; iti — thus; evam — so; niścitya — determining; vai — indeed; dṛḍham — firmly
   The dream is indeed a mental delight; how can I abandon it? So, firmly resolving, I will restrain my mind and see again.
   
   Verse 48
   रुरोध चित्तं तु हठात्तदेतदभवत्‌ स्थिरम्‌ ।
   तदानन्दसमुद्रान्तर्निमग्न इव सोऽभवत्‌ ॥ ४८ ॥
   rurodha cittaṁ tu haṭhāt-tad-etad-abhavat sthiram ।
   tadānanda-samudrāntar-nimagna iva so'bhavat ॥ 48 ॥
   rurodha — restrained; cittam — mind; tu — indeed; haṭhāt — forcefully; tad — that; etat — this; abhavat — became; sthiram — steady; tadā — then; ānanda — of bliss; samudra-antar — ocean within; nimagnaḥ — immersed; iva — as if; saḥ — he; abhavat — became
   He restrained his mind forcefully until it became steady. Then, he felt as if he were immersed in an ocean of inner bliss.
   
   Verse 49
   पुनश्चित्तप्रचलनात्‌ प्रबुद्धोऽभवदञ्जसा ।
   किमेष मेऽभवत्‌ स्वप्नश्चाऽथवा चित्तविभ्रमः ॥ ४९ ॥
   punaś-citta-pracalanāt prabuddho'bhavad-añjasā ।
   kim-eṣa me'bhavat svapnaś-cā'thavā citta-vibhramaḥ ॥ 49 ॥
   punaḥ — again; citta-pracalanāt — by the movement of mind; prabuddhaḥ — awakened; abhavat — became; añjasā — immediately; kim — what; eṣaḥ — this; me — my; abhavat — was; svapnaḥ — dream; ca — and; athavā — or; citta-vibhramaḥ — mental confusion
   With the movement of his mind, he immediately awakened. What was that? Was it a dream or just mental confusion?
   
   Verse 50
   आहोस्वित्‌ सत्य एष स्यादविचिन्त्यं विभाति मे ।
   नाऽन्वभूवं किञ्चिदपि सुखमाप्तं कथं मया ॥ ५० ॥
   āhosvit satya eṣa syād-avicintyaṁ vibhāti me ।
   nā'nvabhūvaṁ kiñcid-api sukham-āptaṁ kathaṁ mayā ॥ 50 ॥
   āhosvit — or; satyaḥ — true; eṣaḥ — this; syāt — may be; avicintyam — inconceivable; vibhāti — appears; me — to me; na — not; anvabhūvam — I experienced; kiñcit — anything; api — even; sukham — bliss; āptam — obtained; katham — how; mayā — by me
   Or is this indeed the truth? It seems inconceivable to me. I have never experienced such bliss before; how did I attain it?
   
   Verse 51
   अहोऽस्य सुखलेशस्य तुल्यं नास्त्यत्र किञ्चन ।
   अहं सुषुप्तवन्मूढः कथमेतत्‌ सुखं स्थितम्‌ ॥ ५१ ॥
   aho'sya sukhaleśasya tulyaṁ nāstyatra kiñcana ।
   ahaṁ suṣuptavan-mūḍhaḥ katham-etat sukhaṁ sthitam ॥ 51 ॥
   aho — oh; asya — of this; sukha-leśasya — a fragment of bliss; tulyam — equal; nāsti — not; atra — here; kiñcana — anything; ahaṁ — I; suṣuptavat — like in deep sleep; mūḍhaḥ — deluded; katham — how; etat — this; sukham — bliss; sthitam — remained
   Oh, nothing here in this world, compares to even a fragment of this bliss. I was deluded, as if in deep sleep; how did this bliss still remain?
   
   Verse 52
   नात्र हेतुं कञ्चिदपि लक्षये तत्‌ कथं भवेत्‌ ।
   आत्मावगमनायाहं प्रवृत्तोऽप्यद्य नाविदम्‌ ॥ ५२ ॥
   nātra hetuṁ kañcid-api lakṣaye tat kathaṁ bhavet ।
   ātmāvagamanāyāhaṁ pravṛtto'py-adya nāvidam ॥ 52 ॥
   na — not; atra — here; hetum — cause; kañcid-api — any; lakṣaye — I perceive; tat — that; katham — how; bhavet — can be; ātmāvagamanāya — for self-realization; ahaṁ — I; pravṛttaḥ — engaged; api — even; adya — today; na — not; avidam — knew
   I do not perceive any cause here; how can that be? Despite my efforts for self-realization, I did not know this until today.
   
   Verse 53
   आत्मानमन्यच्चान्यच्च पश्यामि किमिदं भवेत्‌ ।
   प्रकाशो वान्धकारो वा सुखं वान्यदथापि वा ॥ ५३ ॥
   ātmānam-anyac-cānyac-ca paśyāmi kim-idaṁ bhavet ।
   prakāśo vāndhakāro vā sukhaṁ vānyad-athāpi vā ॥ 53 ॥
   ātmānam — self; anyat — other; ca — and; anyat — other; ca — and; paśyāmi — I see; kim — what; idam — this; bhavet — can be; prakāśaḥ — light; vā — or; andhakāraḥ — darkness; vā — or; sukham — bliss; vā — or; anyat — another; athāpi — or; vā — or
   I see the self, as another, and yet another; what can this be? Is it light or darkness, bliss or something else?
   
   Verse 54
   आत्मा भवेन्मम तथा क्रमिकैतत्स्वरूपकः ।
   नान्तमेम्यत्र भूयस्तां पृच्छामि विदुषीं प्रियाम्‌ ॥ ५४ ॥
   ātmā bhaven-mama tathā kramikaitat-svarūpakaḥ ।
   nāntam-emy-atra bhūyas-tāṁ pṛcchāmi viduṣīṁ priyām ॥ 54 ॥
   ātmā — self; bhavet — may be; mama — mine; tathā — so; kramikā — sequential; etat — this; svarūpakaḥ — form; na — not; antam — end; emy — I reach; atra — here; bhūyaḥ — again; tāṁ — her; pṛcchāmi — I ask; viduṣīm — wise; priyām — dear
   This self may be mine, and this form seems to follow sequentially. I cannot reach a final conclusion here; I will ask my wise, dear one again.
   
   Verse 55
   इति निश्चित्य द्वारेशमाहूयाज्ञां समादिशत्‌ ।
   स्वसन्निधानमानेतुं हेमलेखां नृपात्मजः ॥ ५५ ॥
   iti niścitya dvāreśam-āhūyājñāṁ samādiśat ।
   sva-sannidhānam-ānetuṁ hemalekhāṁ nṛpātmajaḥ ॥ 55 ॥
   iti — thus; niścitya — determining; dvāreśam — doorkeeper; āhūya — calling; ājñām — order; samādiśat — instructed; sva-sannidhānam — to his presence; ānetum — to bring; hemalekhām — Hemalekha; nṛpa-ātmajaḥ — prince
   Thus deciding, the prince called the doorkeeper and instructed him to bring Hemalekha to his presence.
   
   Verse 56
   अथ प्राप्ता मुहूर्तेन द्वारिकस्य निदेशतः ।
   आरुरोह महासौधं मेरुमिन्दुप्रभेव सा ॥ ५६ ॥
   atha prāptā muhūrtena dvārikasya nideśataḥ ।
   āruroha mahāsaudhaṁ merum-induprabheva sā ॥ 56 ॥
   atha — then; prāptā — arrived; muhūrtena — in a moment; dvārikasya — doorkeeper's; nideśataḥ — by order; āruroha — ascended; mahā-saudham — great mansion; merum — Meru mountain; indu-prabhā — moonlight; iva — like; sā — she
   She arrived promptly at the doorkeeper's order and ascended the great mansion that looked like moonlight gracing Mount Meru.
   
   Verse 57
   अथापश्यद्‌ राजसुतं प्रियं शान्तात्ममानसम्‌ ।
   निश्चलं निर्विकारं च संहृतेन्द्रियमण्डलम्‌ ॥ ५७ ॥
   athāpaśyad rāja-sutaṁ priyaṁ śāntātma-mānasam ।
   niścalaṁ nirvikāraṁ ca saṁhṛtendriya-maṇḍalam ॥ 57 ॥
   atha — then; apaśyat — saw; rāja-sutam — prince; priyam — dear; śānta-ātma-mānasam — tranquil-minded; niścalam — steady; nirvikāram — unchanging; ca — and; saṁhṛta-indriya-maṇḍalam — senses withdrawn
   Then she saw the prince, her dear one, with a tranquil mind, steady, unchanging, and with senses withdrawn.
   
   Verse 58
   समीपमुपसृत्याशु तद्विष्टरमुपारुहत्‌ ।
   एकासनोपविष्टायां तस्यां स निमिषार्द्धतः ॥ ५८ ॥
   samīpam-upasṛtyāśu tad-viṣṭaram-upāruhat ।
   ekāsanopaviṣṭāyāṁ tasyāṁ sa nimiṣārdhataḥ ॥ 58 ॥
   samīpam — near; upasṛtya — approaching; āśu — quickly; tad-viṣṭaram — that seat; upāruhat — ascended; eka-āsana-upaviṣṭāyām — sitting on the same seat; tasyām — with her; saḥ — he; nimiṣa-ardhataḥ — in a moment
   Approaching near, she quickly ascended her seat, and she sat beside him in a moment.
   
   Verse 59
   उन्मील्य नयने पार्श्वे समालोकयदास्थिताम्‌ ।
   आलोकिता प्रियं शीघ्रं प्रणयात्‌ परिषस्वजे ॥ ५९ ॥
   unmīlya nayane pārśve samālokayad-āsthitām ।
   ālokitā priyaṁ śīghraṁ praṇayāt pariṣasvaje ॥ 59 ॥
   unmīlya — opening; nayane — eyes; pārśve — side; samālokayat — saw; āsthitām — present; ālokitā — seeing; priyam — dear one; śīghram — quickly; praṇayāt — with affection; pariṣasvaje — embraced
   Opening his eyes, he saw her present by his side. Seeing his dear one, he quickly embraced her with affection.
   
   Verse 60
   ततः प्राहामृतस्यन्दि सुन्दरं वचनं प्रिया ।
   नाथ किं भवताहूता कच्चित्ते नीरुजं तनौ ॥ ६० ॥
   tataḥ prāhāmṛta-syandi sundaraṁ vacanaṁ priyā ।
   nātha kiṁ bhavatā-hūtā kaccit-te nīrujaṁ tanau ॥ 60 ॥
   tataḥ — then; prāha — spoke; amṛta-syandi — nectar-flowing; sundaram — beautiful; vacanam — words; priyā — dear one; nātha — lord; kim — why; bhavatā — by you; āhūtā — called; kaccit — is; te — your; nīrujam — healthy; tanau — body
   Then his dear one spoke beautiful, nectar-like words, "My lord, why have you called me? Is your body healthy?"
   
   Verse 61
   वदाहूतौ कारणं मे यदर्थमहमागता ।
   एवं प्रियानुयुक्तः स बभाषे स्वात्मनः प्रियाम्‌ ॥ ६१ ॥
   vadāhūtau kāraṇaṁ me yadarthamahamāgatā ।
   evaṁ priyānuyuktaḥ sa babhāṣe svātmanaḥ priyām ॥ 61 ॥
   vada — tell; āhūtau — called; kāraṇam — reason; me — to me; yadartham — for what reason; aham — I; āgatā — have come; evaṁ — thus; priyā — dear; anuyuktaḥ — asked; saḥ — he; babhāṣe — spoke; svātmanaḥ — himself; priyām — to the dear one
   Tell me the reason you called me, for which I have come. Thus asked by his dear one, he spoke to her about his experiences.
   
   Verse 62
   प्रिये त्वयानुशिष्टोऽहं विविक्तेऽत्र समास्थितः ।
   विचारपरमः स्वात्मरूपलक्षणहेतवे ॥ ६२ ॥
   priye tvayānuśiṣṭo'haṁ vivikte'tra samāsthitaḥ ।
   vicāra-paramaḥ svātma-rūpa-lakṣaṇa-hetave ॥ 62 ॥
   priye — dear; tvayā — by you; anuśiṣṭaḥ — instructed; aham — I; vivikte — in solitude; atra — here; samāsthitaḥ — have settled; vicāra-paramaḥ — deeply thinking; svātma — self; rūpa — form; lakṣaṇa — characteristic; hetave — for the reason
   Dear, as you instructed, I have settled here in solitude, deeply contemplating the nature and characteristics of the self.
   
   Verse 63
   तत्परेणापि चित्रं तु लक्षितं तत्‌ पृथक्‌ किमु ।
   आत्मनः सर्वदा प्राप्तेर्भासमानत्वतोऽपि च ॥ ६३ ॥
   tat-pareṇāpi citraṁ tu lakṣitaṁ tat pṛthak kimu ।
   ātmanaḥ sarvadā prāpterbhāsamānatvato'pi ca॥ 63 ॥
   tat — that; pareṇa — further; api — even; citram — strange; tu — indeed; lakṣitam — observed; tat — that; pṛthak — separate; kimu — why; ātmanaḥ — of the self; sarvadā — always; prāpteḥ — present; bhāsamānatvataḥ — due to being manifest; api — also; ca — and
   Furthermore, it is strange that it is observed as separate; why is that? The self is always present and manifest.
   
   Verse 64
   असम्यग्‌ भासनं चान्यभासनस्य निमित्ततः ।
   इति मत्वा निरुध्यान्यभासनं सुव्यवस्थितः ॥ ६४ ॥
   asamyaḍ bhāsanaṁ cānyabhāsanasya nimittataḥ ।
